France and Germany Reach a Compromise: Saar Plebiscite Date Decided; To Be Held on January 13 Next Year; Citizens' Security Guaranteed 39

(Geneva) The Saar plebiscite issue has recently been resolved after repeated consultations between representatives of France, Germany, and Italy. The date of the vote has been set for January 13, 1935, the earliest possible date next year. This solution was reached after first determining the security of the Saar residents and then deciding on the date. Saar voters will be guaranteed by the League of Nations, regardless of which country the Saar territory belongs to in the future. According to the compromise reached this time, neither the German state, its agencies, nor its civil servants shall take retaliatory action or discriminate against voters after the vote. If, after this clear reinstatement, there are still people who treat voters in the aforementioned ways, the victims can file a complaint with the "Voting Court" within one year. This court will be located in the Saar for the first year, and then its functions will be performed by the League of Nations Administrative Council and the Permanent Court of Arbitration at The Hague, with no expiration date. (1st Havas)

(Geneva) A conference between Germany and France, previously mediated by Italy, has reached a complete agreement after several days of mediation. The agreement has now been approved by the German government, setting January 13, 1935, as the date for the Saar region's plebiscite. This date is also the latest possible date stipulated by the Treaty of Versailles. Other matters in the agreement stipulate that the police force during the voting period shall be entirely composed of Saar residents, and foreign senior police officers may only be added in times of danger. Both Germany and France guarantee the absolute freedom of voting, prohibiting all retaliatory actions, but only legal residents of the Saar region are included, while expatriates currently residing in the Saar are not. However, the League of Nations Council still has the right to expand the scope of guarantees in the future. In addition, a special international court will be organized during the voting period to hear various voting cases within three months after the vote. (1st National Telegram)

(Geneva) Today, the Associated Press received news from reliable sources in France and Germany confirming that the Saar self-determination vote will be held on January 13, 1935. Opponents of Hitler in the Saar region strongly advocate postponing the self-determination vote, arguing that the National Socialist Party's agitation of terror and retaliation movements prevents people from voting freely. However, the League of Nations has decided to hold the self-determination vote according to the original date. The Saar Governing Commission and French and German diplomats have agreed on the following measures for the self-determination vote: (1) The two governments promise to avoid threats, retaliation, or discrimination, and prohibit their representatives or people from adopting these measures. (2) If citizens of the Saar region are harmed by retaliation, they may appeal to the Voting Court. This court will be maintained until one year after the vote, after which people may appeal to the League of Nations Administrative Council or the International Court of Justice in The Hague. (3) No international police may be stationed in the Saar region. If the International Administrative Council deems it necessary, these police must be recruited in Luxembourg. (1st National Telegram)

League of Nations Administrative Council to Meet Today to Discuss Hungarian-Yugoslav Dispute 40

(Cairo) The League of Nations Administrative Council is scheduled to meet on Monday to discuss the border dispute between Hungary and Yugoslavia. This day coincides with the anniversary of the signing of the Treaty of Trianon (i.e., the treaty of peace between the Allied Powers and Hungary). Hungarian Prime Minister Gömbös's mouthpiece, the "Függetlenség" newspaper, pointed out the coincidence of this date, but said that Hungary does not want to provoke political disputes and only seeks a clear resolution to the various border disputes that have accumulated over time and become unbearable. (2nd Havas)

Blocking Munitions to Bolivia and Paraguay: A Political, Not Legal, Matter; Jurists Believe It Impractical 41

(Geneva) The League of Nations had commissioned a special committee of legal experts to study the substantive issues of blocking munitions to Paraguay and Bolivia. According to their conclusion today, the case is unlikely to be implemented. Germany's Law to Expel Foreigners Takes Effect Yesterday 42

(Berlin) President Hindenburg met with Chancellor Hitler today to discuss various current political issues, with particular emphasis on disarmament. The law on the expulsion of foreigners, passed on March 23 of this year, came into effect today. Foreigners or stateless persons may be expelled by order of the local (formerly state) political police. In addition to foreigners subject to expulsion under current laws, including those who have committed minor or major crimes, the new law stipulates other circumstances, such as foreigners whose behavior endangers German diplomacy, damages public morals, or fail to pay rent, customs duties, or violate currency laws. Foreigners who are beggars or vagrants may also be expelled at the request of public relief agencies. (2nd Havas Telegram)

International Silk Association Convenes to Boycott Asian Silk 43

The International Silk Association of Lyon convened here, mentioning the issue of competition from the silk industries of Asian countries. It was believed that the current situation is serious, and it is insufficient to reverse the decline without the united cooperation of countries with similar working conditions. The association earnestly requested all attending groups to do their utmost to find ways to jointly resist the import of Asian silk products. In particular, attention should be paid to striving to develop the consumption of silk produced in Europe. (1st Havas Telegram)

Senate Abolition Bill Vetoed by Southern Ireland's Senate, But Can Still Become Law After One Year 44

⊙ Dublin The Senate today vetoed the bill to abolish the Senate by a vote of 33 to 15. The opposition vigorously attacked the bill in the meeting. Minister of Lands, Mr. Connolly, representing the government, answered questions, accusing the Senate of undermining the government's legislation. It is claimed that the Irish people have accepted the Anglo-Irish Treaty as a cornerstone of national liberation, and the government does not want to hesitate along the way, causing unnecessary delays in the establishment of the Irish Republic. Mr. de Valera then stated that this bill would allow the Irish to advance along the path they have decided. Although the bill was vetoed by the Senate today, it can automatically become law after one year. (1st Reuters Telegram)

Drought and Fires in America 45

(New York) Forest areas in Maine, USA, which are popular vacation destinations, suddenly caught fire today, destroying 25 houses. 2,500 firefighters are engaged in firefighting. St. Louis, Missouri, experienced thunderstorms today with six cases of fires caused by electrical strikes. The drought has not subsided, and fires have broken out again, causing immense hardship. In Illinois, the temperature in the shade reached 124 degrees, and a certain rice field spontaneously combusted. The Governor of New York today closed all traffic in the state's forests until the fire-prone period has passed. Butte, Montana, suddenly experienced thunderstorms, and traffic was suspended. According to news from Winnipeg, Canada, thousands of acres of grassland in Manitoba have been destroyed by locusts. (2nd Reuters Telegram)

⊙ Chicago After a long drought, this area has experienced unprecedented heat. Today, at least ten people died from the heat in the Midwest. Millions of people are seeking refuge in the water, and several have drowned as a result. Some smaller beaches are so crowded that police had to be called in to maintain order. The high temperatures in the cities of the Midwest are unprecedented for May and June, and even exceed the heat waves of mid-August. According to private estimates, this year's wheat harvest will be the smallest since 1907. Many farmers will be completely bankrupt. In recent days, locusts have bred more and more severely. Airplanes are being used today to control them. The highest recorded temperatures were 102 degrees Fahrenheit in Chicago and 108 degrees in Milwaukee. Businesses selling ice and cold drinks in various places have tripled their profits and are feeling a shortage of manpower. Swimming pools are also overcrowded. (1st National Telegram)

Serious Labor Unrest in America 46

(Washington) The President's desk is piled high today with letters and telegrams from all over the country calling on President Roosevelt to personally mediate labor disputes, as the failure to resolve the labor unrest in various places quickly will bring a large portion of American industry to a standstill. Labor leaders are confident that the President will return to the White House from New York on Monday and make every effort to mediate the steel and textile industries labor disputes, as there are approximately one million workers involved in these two industries. They believe that Roosevelt will hold negotiations similar to those that recently prevented a general strike in the automotive industry, at which time the President had detailed discussions with leaders from both labor and management, with satisfactory results. Some members of the steelworkers' union claim that unless the President fulfills his promise to implement the unconditional collective bargaining clause in the steel code, a general strike will be implemented next week. Textile workers also say that if the Reconstruction Administration does not change its order to reduce working hours by a quarter or find other ways to compensate, they will also strike. The White House has also received a request from the Toledo Central Labor Union to prevent a general strike and newly occurred riots and bloodshed in that area. As for the strike at the electrical factory, labor and management are very insistent and there is no solution. (30th National Telegram) ⊙ The Toledo Central Labor Union today asked President Roosevelt to intervene in or find a way to prevent the planned general strike in the Toledo automotive industry in Ohio. The general strike was approved by 68 of the 103 unions and is scheduled to begin today. (1st Reuters Telegram)

(Washington) After negotiations between the Reconstruction Administration and both labor and management, it is now claimed that the general strike of 300,000 textile workers is definitely able to be quelled. General Johnson, Director of the Reconstruction Administration, officially announced this afternoon that the terms of the settlement remain secret and will be announced tomorrow. (1st National Telegram)

Another Severe Earthquake in India: Walls Collapse, No Casualties Yet, Residents Like Birds Frightened by a Bow 47

⊙ Calcutta The town of Madhepura in the Bihar and Orissa province of India, a thriving area along the railway, was hit by a severe earthquake at midnight yesterday. All buildings were shaken. The area suffered an earthquake in January of this year, killing 1,500 people. Residents still had lingering fears, so they all ran into the streets in their sleeping clothes. Houses damaged by the previous earthquake suffered further damage from last night's quake, with many walls collapsing. Fortunately, everyone had escaped during the initial tremor, so there were no casualties. Thunder and rain occurred at the time, making the people even more miserable. According to records from the Alipore Observatory, the epicenter was located 370 miles north of Bihar. (2nd Reuters Telegram)

Bread Shortage in Soviet Russia Causes Prices to Soar 48

(Moscow) The price of white bread in Moscow suddenly rose by 120% today, and the price of black bread rose by 100%, due to a prolonged drought in wheat-producing areas. Last spring's famine in Soviet Russia caused millions to starve to death. Recent rainfall may prevent a recurrence of the tragedy, but people in some areas are already suffering from edema due to hunger. (1st Reuters Telegram)

Economic Commission to Build the Beijing-Shandong Railway 54

(Nanjing) In order to connect the transportation of Jiangsu, Anhui, and Shandong provinces, the Economic Commission previously planned to build a highway from Pukou to Tiangchang in eastern Anhui, Qingjiangpu in northern Jiangsu, Pixian, and Tancheng in southern Shandong. It is now learned that the commission has changed its plan and will convert the highway into a railway, named the Beijing-Shandong Railway. An engineering committee has been established in Nanjing, dividing the entire route into four sections: one from Pukou to Tiangchang County, one from Tiangchang County to Qingjiangpu, one from Qingjiangpu to Pixian, and one from Pixian to Tancheng, which will be surveyed separately. Currently, the Pukou-Tiangchang section has been surveyed by the engineering committee, and construction will begin within days. The surveying work for the Tiangchang-Qingjiang section has not yet been completed and will be postponed until the end of this month before work can begin. As for the two sections from Qingjiangpu via Siyang and Rugao to Pixian and even to Tancheng in Shandong, they also need to be surveyed. The Jiangsu Provincial Government has been consulted to send personnel to survey. The Jiangsu Construction Department has now dispatched a special commissioner Yu and a surveying team to depart from Pukou, with the endpoint within Pixian. The area north of Pixian has entered Shandong, and the Shandong Provincial Government will dispatch personnel to survey. The project is expected to be completed by next spring. (2nd Special Telegram)

The Scope of the General Office of the Academia Sinica Is Reduced 60

(Nanjing) Ding Wenjiang, Director-General of the Academia Sinica, concurrently serves as a professor at Peking University, and originally had to come to Nanjing to take office after the end of the semester. He came to Shanghai at the invitation of President Cai last month and came to Nanjing from Shanghai on the 18th and took office at the General Office of the Academia Sinica on the 21st. Because there are still unfinished matters in Peiping, he still has to go to Peiping and is scheduled to return to Nanjing to take charge on the 8th. It is planned to have a method in the institute's future plans. From next year, the scope of the institute's General Office will be reduced. The original four departments of Documents, Accounting, General Affairs, and International Exchange of Publications will all be abolished except for the Accounting Department, which will remain the same. The Documents Department will be replaced by three secretaries, the General Affairs Department will be replaced by one or two general affairs staff, and the International Exchange of Publications Department will be transferred to the Ministry of Education. The remaining affiliated institutions, such as the nine research institutes of Physics, Chemistry, Engineering, Geology, Astronomy, Meteorology, Psychology, History, Linguistics, and Social Sciences, will all remain the same. However, the Natural History Museum will be changed to the Institute of Biology, with Mr. Wang internally appointed as the director. The addresses of the various institutes will remain the same, except for the Institute of History and Linguistics, which will be moved to Nanjing. Ding believes that the institute has had financial difficulties in recent years and will strive to save money and reduce the budget in the future, so the organization will be simplified. (2nd Special Telegram)

International Commercial Telegram - Special Commercial Report from Reuters, June 2nd 88

Gold and Silver London Prices: This morning, the London gold price was 137 shillings and two pence, half a penny higher than yesterday's price.

London bar silver prices fell by 0.0625, with spot quotes at 19 pence 4375, and futures at 19 pence and a half. The market was uneventful, with very little trading.

The New York bar silver market opened weak, following the London telegram. Merchants are now awaiting developments in Washington. Interest in the market is very low, and sentiment is mixed. Today's forward opening prices, except for March, which increased by five points, contracted by varying amounts, from seven to sixteen points.

Exchange Rates 89

Sterling-Dollar: The London foreign exchange market was quiet this morning, with no sign of official intervention to stabilize exchange rates. The opening price for the sterling-dollar exchange rate was $5.06625, the same as yesterday's closing price. It later rose by 0.1875 to $5.068125, but the price fell near closing, so the closing price was $5.065625, which was 0.0625 lower than this morning's opening price. Also, one U.S. dollar equals three shillings and eleven pence and 378.

Sterling-Franc: The opening price fell by seven points to 76.96 francs. The closing price fell another six points to 77.90 francs.

Dollar-Sterling: Today's opening price for the dollar-sterling exchange rate was $5.0675, which was 0.125 higher than yesterday's closing price. It later fell to $5.0625, but then quickly recovered to $5.0675, the same as the opening price.

Dollar-Franc: The opening price for the dollar-franc exchange rate was 6.58 and three-quarters, up by three-quarters.

Cotton and Wheat 90

American Cotton: The cotton market opened firm, with concerns about early drought and signs of resolution in the textile industry labor strike. Domestic and international parties and speculators successively bought in, causing prices to rise.

British Cotton: The closing price for July futures in the Liverpool cotton market was 6.18, up eight points.

British Wheat: The closing price for July futures in the Liverpool wheat market was four shillings and nine and three-quarter pence, down one and a half pence.

Rubber 91

The London rubber market opened firm but closed weak. The trading price for July and September futures was 6.375 pence, the same as yesterday's price.

The New York rubber market was affected by the weak closing of the London rubber market. The opening price for futures was slightly lower. Some profit-taking and selling by dealers was absorbed by retail buyers.

Securities 92

The New York securities market opened weak today, with most stock prices falling, with a maximum drop of one point. Railway and public utility stocks were particularly under pressure. Labor unrest and lack of confidence, as well as the uncertain implementation of the Securities Exchange Act, were causes of anxiety. The volume of transactions in the first hour this morning was 240,000 shares. The following is a report from Jardine Matheson & Co. on the prices of 15 New York securities (as of 10:45 AM):

Eastern Route Army Captures Shuikou, Southern Route Can Soon Capture Huichang 100

A dispatch from Nanchang states that the military operations to suppress bandits have been consistently victorious. The complete bandit areas in Jiangxi Province consist of only six counties: Ruijin, Huichang, Xingguo, Ningdu, Yudu, and Shicheng. In Fujian, they consist of only Tingzhou, Liancheng, Ninghua, and other counties and semi-bandit areas near those counties. The various routes of the National Army are currently recovering the semi-bandit areas and then clearing out the bandits. Some time ago, the Eastern Route Army under Jiang Dingwen advanced on Tinglian. Now, military reports say that Shuikou, located 60 li from Tingcheng, has been captured. The bandits have built fortifications north of Tinglian, where there is expected to be a fierce battle. As for the Southern Route Army, after capturing Junmenling, in addition to assigning certain units to garrison Yangjiaoying, Luotang, and Junmenling to strictly guard against the Ye Jianying bandit's return attack, the remaining forces are advancing on Huichang via different routes. The Li Zhenqiu units have reached the Yushui area, several dozen li from Huichang, and the city of Huichang is expected to fall soon. After the Northern Route Army recovered Guangchang and Longgang, they approached Ningdu and Xingguo. It is reported that a certain unit has crossed Guangchang to take Shicheng, advancing in tandem with the Eastern Route Army, which is taking Ninghua from Jianning. Another unit is flanking Wangpo Xiaopu, joining forces with a certain route army that has reached Longgang to attack Ningdu. The Western Route Army is actively clearing out the fleeing remnants of Xiao Ke, Cai Huiwen, and Kong Hechong along the west bank of the Gan River to avoid any constraints. At the same time, certain units are ordered to build fortifications along the Gan River in the Wan'an, Taihe, and Ji'an areas to strengthen the blockade. Because the Red bandits are now surrounded by the armies of four provinces, they have a plan to break through a bloody path from Xingguo, break through the Gan River from Wan'an and Taihe, escape the encirclement, and seek a new way out. The Western Route Army must make arrangements to defend and block on both sides of the Gan River. (May 31st)

The Rising Momentum of the Volunteer Army in Western Liaoning: An'tu County Surrounded and Expected to Fall Soon; The Volunteer Army in Ji'an and Huanren Counties Has Strong Resolve; The Volunteer Army at Sandaohe Killed Many Japanese Soldiers 101

A dispatch from Shenyang reports that the various volunteer armies in the counties of An'tu, Ji'an, Huanren, and the Sandaohe area in western Liaoning are actively operating. The Japanese Kwantung Army dispatched the Morita, Hamamoto, and Saito regiments to attack, suffering repeated heavy losses. Over 50 Japanese officers and soldiers were killed or wounded. The leader of the volunteer army besieging An'tu and Ji'an counties, nicknamed "Loyal Hero," is extremely resolute in his will to punish the puppets and resist Japan. The following is a detailed account of the volunteer army's resistance against the enemy:

In the Sandaohe area of western Liaoning, over 700 volunteer soldiers suddenly appeared. Upon hearing the news, the Japanese Kwantung Army immediately dispatched the Morita unit, consisting of over 300 soldiers, to Sandaohe Bamian, located 10 li south of Tong, on a military train on May 26th. By about 3:00 PM, they began engaging the volunteer army in that area. The volunteer army launched a fierce attack, and the battle lasted until late at night. Because the Japanese army was unfamiliar with the terrain, they were flanked by the volunteer army, which encircled them for several hours. Over 20 Japanese soldiers were killed, and five machine guns, over 30 rifles, and a large amount of ammunition were seized. Over 1,000 volunteer soldiers, whom the Japanese call the "Red Army," were discovered in the Xiaoshahe area northwest of An'tu County. This volunteer army operates swiftly, is well-equipped with ammunition, and has new weapons. On the 24th of last month, they occupied Dashahe. On the 26th, they advanced towards Huanghezi. They are currently planning to capture An'tu County, and the Japanese puppet army and police are on high alert.

The volunteer army leaders, nicknamed "Fairness" and "Loyal Hero," who are lurking in the Gaoliyingzi area of Ji'an County and the Lichagou area of Huanren County, have each led their respective units of over 500 soldiers to take unified action to capture Ji'an County in an attempt to launch a major operation. Small groups of volunteer soldiers are responding to the call every day. The leaders have declared that they have nothing to fear from the Japanese puppet army. On the 21st, the Japanese army dispatched the Hamamoto company and the Saito regiment to attack, engaging in fierce battles for a day and a night, killing Japanese officers Lieutenant Kurokawa Yukio and Second Lieutenant Ichino Yukifuku, as well as over ten soldiers. The volunteer army also suffered over ten casualties. (Northeast News Agency)

Internal Split Among the Jiangxi Bandits: Zhou Enlai and Peng Dehuai Have Conflicting Opinions on Military Strategy; The Eighth Division of the Southern Route Army Captures the Qianfeng Ao Bandit Stronghold 102

A dispatch from Guangzhou reports that the communist bandits in eastern Jiangxi have suffered significant losses since their defeat at Junmen. Recently, the Eastern Route Army has been closing in on Changting, and the First and Second Columns of the Southern Route Army have established contact, imposing a strict blockade on Huichang, Yudu, and other areas. As a result, the communist bandit leaders have been holding meetings for several days, urgently seeking ways to flee. According to military news, the remaining communists in Jiangxi, recently realizing that the environment is becoming increasingly dangerous, have decided to implement their plan to avoid the strong and attack the weak, concentrating their forces in one corner. If the Eastern and Southern Route Armies press forward, they plan to cross into western Jiangxi, joining forces with the remaining bandits in eastern Hunan and along the Yangtze River to prolong their existence. The communist bandit leaders recently held a meeting in Ruijin. Zhou Enlai, Chairman of the Communist Bandit Puppet Military Commission, strongly advocated for this proposal. His reason was that the natural barrier of Junmen had been lost, and the defenses of the bandit areas of Huichang and Ruijin had been dismantled. If the National Army were to surround them from all sides, they would have no way out. They plan to first focus on one route of bandit troops in order to break through and preserve some remaining strength. However, the bandit leaders Luo Binghui and Peng Dehuai believe that the western Jiangxi region is barren and difficult to develop. They plan to invade northern Fujian or seek to enter Zhejiang Province. Internal opinions are highly divided.

The First and Second Columns of the Southern Route Army have recently increased their troop strength on the front lines, and the heavy artillery unit of the Shidivision has been deployed to the front lines. The communist bandits will be hard-pressed to launch a counterattack. South of Junmen, they are actively handling the aftermath, rushing to set up anti-communist groups and conducting strict household registration to prevent the remnants of the bandits from blending in. All grains, kerosene, salt, and other items in the area are prohibited from being sold out of the area to supply the bandits. The supply of salt is distributed according to the people's registration book, with each person receiving three qian per day to limit consumption. As for food, public sales offices are also established to implement public sales. Refugees who return must register in the Baojia system and implement the five-household mutual guarantee system to prevent malfeasance. As for the units on the front lines, before launching a major offensive, they are striving to search for remnants of bandits to avoid leaving future troubles. On the 21st of this month, it was discovered that there were over 1,000 bandits entrenched in Qianfeng Ao, north of Junmen. The 22nd and 24th Regiments of the Eighth Division were dispatched to surround the area. From 9:00 AM, they began bombarding the Qianfeng Ao bandit stronghold, and by 11:00 AM, they had captured the stronghold. The remaining bandits retreated towards Qingxi. On the 23rd, the Kou Division, stationed near Gan County, discovered a communist bandit puppet guerrilla battalion in Datian. They dispatched the Zeng Zhaoji battalion of the teaching regiment and the Hualin Temple reserve team to cross the river and surround and suppress them. The puppet battalion commander, Zhong Decai, and nine others were captured, and over 100 villagers who had been coerced into service by the bandits were rescued. Also, on the 21st, the First Division, stationed at Chongshiwei, received a report that hundreds of bandits from the Bao Wei Ju puppet guerrilla team were massacring wealthy farmers near Gaopai. They immediately dispatched the Wen and Liang battalions to suppress them overnight. As a result, three bandit leaders were killed, and over 200 hostages were rescued. The National Army is still searching the area. (May 28th)

He Long and Xu Xiangqian's Two Forces Have Both Become Desperate Gangs 103

Chen Wanren telegraphed that the He bandits had collapsed without forming a proper army; Tang Shizun reported that the Xu bandits had become fish in a cauldron. A dispatch from Chengdu reports that the He bandits previously crossed into Pengshui in eastern Sichuan, where they were severely attacked by the Chen Division of the 21st Army, which cut the bandits into several segments, rendering them unable to form a proper army. Yesterday, Chen Dunren, the division commander of that division, telegraphed the Anfu Committee to report on the progress of the suppression. The following is an excerpt:

"To the Chengdu Anfu Committee, regarding the He bandits' invasion of the You area, my unit was ordered to reinforce the area with two regiments of troops, deployed to the right of Guizhou to prevent them from crossing and disrupting the southern bank. At the same time, two regiments of troops were sent to reinforce the Tian unit to encircle and suppress the bandits. Seeing that we were prepared and knowing that they could not succeed, the bandits first crossed from the Guizhou territory to Xiaodong in Zhonglu, and then crossed to Youyang. I immediately ordered the Xu and Chen regiments to pursue them and cooperate with the Tian unit to encircle and suppress them. They had already driven the bandits to their old nest in Baihu Village and Caishengou, near the intersection of Sichuan, Hunan, and Hubei. Because the troops in Hunan and Hubei were blocking them tightly, the bandits changed their plan, taking advantage of the weakness of our rear defense, and rushed towards Pengshui day and night. At that time, Pengcheng was in the rear, and its defenses were weak, so it was taken by the bandits. Fortunately, my Xu and Chen regiments followed closely, and reinforcements were sent from the rear of Fuling, commanded by Da Brigade, to intercept and suppress them. The bandits then abandoned the city and crossed the river, fleeing towards Huangjiaba. Our army followed again, striking the bandits at the Shimaoba area, forty li from Guizhou Province, dividing the bandits into several segments and dispersing them towards Houping. There are no bandit traces in Sichuan. I am now notifying the troops stationed in Guizhou Province to intercept and suppress them, striving to annihilate them completely and eliminate future troubles. In this battle, the officers and soldiers of the two companies of my garrison in Peng County fought against the bandits, outnumbered but not outmatched, with many killed or wounded. Battalion Commander Shao Hua of the Xian Battalion committed suicide by jumping into the river after being injured out of anger. Several staff members and local gentry were also taken away. After the recovery, I ordered the Xu Regiment to cooperate with the county government to investigate and report the losses. According to the telegram, after the recovery of Pengcheng, a detailed investigation revealed that most of the company and platoon leaders, soldiers, and civilians of the Xian Battalion were killed or wounded. When the bandits retreated, they also took away Vice Chairman Ning Xiangru and over ten gentry and merchants. Public and private losses amounted to over 100,000, and so on. In addition to ordering proper consolation and finding ways to rescue the kidnapped persons as soon as possible, I am sending this telegram to Chen. Chen Wanren, signed with seal."

Tang Shizun also reported on the bandit suppression situation: "Since being encircled and suppressed by various armies, the Xu bandits have suffered repeated heavy losses and have become exhausted. They are like fish in a cauldron, and their capture is imminent. However, it is an ancient saying that one should not pursue desperate foes. Just like suppressing bandits in Jiangxi, although we have already surrounded them, we are advancing steadily, without rushing forward easily. Observing their tactics, it seems that they are imitating the French method of encircling and suppressing Moroccan rebels in recent years, building roads on all sides to surround them in mountainous areas with inconvenient transportation, so that there will be no problems of insufficient transportation or ineffective mobilization. Thus, we can turn a difficult situation into an advantageous one, gaining momentum, while the bandits will become turtles in a jar. I believe that this method is very good. Not only has Chairman Chiang used it effectively, but we should also learn from it in Sichuan to suppress bandits, ensuring that our transportation and supply are not difficult, and then the Red bandits will be easily annihilated. As for how to suppress bandits, it is a military secret and cannot be announced," and so on. (National News Agency)

Panic Withdrawals at Hunan Provincial Bank: Traitors Create Rumors to Manipulate the Market; The Withdrawals at the Provincial Bank are Gradually Subsiding 104

A dispatch from Changsha reports that Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi flew from Hankou to Hunan last week but left after only a few hours. His hasty movements have led to much speculation among the people of Hunan. Recently, He Jian also left the province by boat on the evening of the 25th for Hankou, then transferred to Jiangxi to visit Chiang Kai-shek. At the same time, his son-in-law, Li Jue (currently the commander of the 19th Division and acting commander of the Hunan Provincial Security Force in southern Hunan), was also summoned to Jiangxi by telegram from Chiang Kai-shek to attend the ten-province security conference. As a result, rumors are rampant, and the market is in turmoil. This has affected the Hunan Provincial Bank, leading to panic withdrawals. Ignorant citizens are rushing to cash their banknotes or even refusing to use them. The bank's banknotes circulating in the market are divided into six denominations: 10 cents, 20 cents, 50 cents, 1 yuan, 5 yuan, and 10 yuan, with a total circulation of approximately 4 million yuan, circulating throughout Hunan Province and the western Jiangxi counties. It has always been fully backed by reserves. After the panic withdrawals began on the 28th, the bank manager, Zhao Heng, not only ordered the bank to redeem banknotes without restriction but also entrusted various banks and major money shops to redeem them on its behalf. At the same time, he also had 500,000 yuan in silver stored in Hankou and over 1 million yuan in silver stored in the exchange offices in various counties transported to the Changsha head office on the 29th to meet the demands for redemption. Meanwhile, Hu Da, the commander of the Changsha Garrison, issued an order strictly prohibiting the spread of rumors, and the provincial government issued an order to all counties and cities not to refuse to accept banknotes from the Provincial Bank to facilitate circulation. By the morning of the 30th, there were fewer people withdrawing money than in the previous two days, and the panic may have subsided. A total of 700,000 to 800,000 yuan in cash has been redeemed. Cao Dianqiu, the acting chairman of the provincial government, scheduled a meeting with reporters at the provincial government guest house at 1:00 PM on the afternoon of the 30th to explain the rumors and reassure the people. According to Cao Dianqiu, Minister Kong's previous visit to Hunan was indeed to inspect the national taxes of Hunan Province, and there were no other incidents. He Jian and Deputy Commander Li's trip to Jiangxi this time was to attend a meeting summoned by Chairman Chiang, and their families traveled with them to Shanghai for medical treatment, which was purely coincidental and had no other implications. There were also rumors that Deputy Commander Zhang's Northeast Army would enter Hunan, which are even more unfounded. According to reports, the current rumors were created by a small number of unscrupulous merchants in the financial sector, hoping to take advantage of this opportunity to speculate and disrupt the market and financial situation in order to manipulate the rise and fall of exchange rates. They only cared about their personal gain, disregarding the disruption of market order and security, which is truly despicable. Military and police agencies have been ordered to investigate and arrest them strictly. Once caught, they will be prosecuted by military law. The following are the telegram from the provincial government to all counties and bureaus not to refuse to use banknotes and the training order from the provincial garrison headquarters prohibiting rumors: (1) Telegram from the provincial government on circulating banknotes: (1) To the mayor of Changsha City and the county magistrates of all counties: The Hunan Provincial Bank has issued various banknotes with sufficient reserves and is ready to redeem them at any time. Its credit has long been established. Recently, during the tense period of the suppression operations, it is heard that there are traitors and bandits who are creating rumors to undermine and disrupt the financial situation and endanger security. In addition to ordering strict investigation and punishment, if it is found that any county or city is creating rumors to suppress or discount the aforementioned banknotes or refusing to accept them, they must be investigated and severely punished without any negligence or leniency, and the telegram must be immediately posted. Seal of He Jian, Chairman of the Hunan Provincial Government. (2) To the directors of all tax bureaus and the inspectors of all grain and rice offices (omitted above): When paying taxes, the bureau must accept the aforementioned banknotes as much as possible, and no corrupt staff should be allowed to suppress or refuse them, lest they be investigated. Seal of He Jian, Chairman of the Hunan Provincial Government. (2) Garrison Command Training Order to Investigate and Prohibit Rumors: Recently, rumors have been rampant in the city, with various versions circulating. People are imagining things and gossiping in the streets. Upon investigation, there is no factual basis. Those who are clear-minded can easily see that these rumors are unfounded, but the citizens are unaware and are being misled and causing unnecessary trouble. In this situation, it is clear that there are lawless scoundrels mixed in with the common people, creating rumors and confusing the public. If we do not investigate the root cause and punish them severely, it will not be enough to punish the traitors and maintain security. In addition to issuing an order, I hereby order you to comply with and supervise your subordinates to conduct a strict investigation. If you encounter anyone spreading rumors or inquiring about information, arrest them immediately and send them to the department for strict investigation. Once the true situation is obtained, all personnel involved in the effort will be rewarded generously. This matter is of great importance, and you must carry it out earnestly without any leniency. Be sure to comply with this order. (May 30th)

Trends in the Tea Industry in Anhui Province: The Overseas Market is Weak, and the Future of the Tea Market is Pessimistic 105

A dispatch from Wuyuan reports that Anhui's Qimen black tea, Zhi De black tea, and Wuyuan Tunxi Shexian green tea have excellent quality and abundance, surpassing the rest of the country, and are the highest-grade teas exported in chests by foreign firms. They have a long history in the overseas market and enjoy a superior position. Wuyuan's "chouxin" tea and Qimen's tribute tea are particularly rare. In the years when the tea market was prosperous, the people of Anhui relied on this naturally abundant and superior specialty for clothing and food. The source of social and economic prosperity was also able to flow steadily without drying up. Unfortunately, prosperity and decline are impermanent. In recent years, the global economic panic has had a severe impact, and the overseas market has undergone drastic changes. Market prices have collapsed, and the trend is rapidly declining. The rural economy, which relies on tea for its livelihood, is on the verge of bankruptcy. The golden age of the past can no longer be sustained. The so-called natural specialty is becoming exhausted. This year's new teas in Anhui Province are about to be launched. The trend of the tea market this year can be glimpsed at this time. The production, quality, mountain prices, firm names, and foreign sales are described in sections to inform readers who are concerned about the tea industry.

Production Losses 106

Anhui Province has the earliest history of tea production. The largest output is in Qimen, Wuyuan, Shexian, and Xiuning, followed by Huo County, and then by other counties. The total tea-planting area in Anhui Province accounts for more than one-third of the paddy fields. Because it is related to their livelihood for the year, farmers regard tea as an important secondary industry and do their best to cultivate and fertilize it. In years of bumper harvests, there are approximately 150,000 dan or more of dried tea, worth over 10 million silver dollars. This year, the tea trees on the plains and shady mountain areas in various counties were affected by the heavy snow and severe cold last winter, and most of them were frozen and withered, hindering their growth. According to the latest estimates after the completion of harvesting and processing by various mountain households, there are widespread reports of losses. On average, it is estimated that there are only 120,000 dan, a decrease of about 30,000 dan compared to the past. This huge amount of decline is unprecedented in recent years.

Tea Quality Still Good 107

Tea from Anhui province, due to the suitability of its soil and climate, has a quality and flavor superior to that of other provinces. However, the superiority or inferiority of the product changes with the smoothness or adversity of the weather during the new tea plucking season. If, when the tea plant develops, there is much rain and sudden heat, the tea buds will burst forth, and small households will be unable to pick and process them in time, easily leading to withering and aging. If the tea leaves are saturated with rain and cannot be exposed to morning dew, the leaves will be hard and the quality light. Even if tea firms refine this type of product, it will be difficult to make fine tea because the raw materials have already been damaged. If foreign merchants have urgent needs, there may be a chance to get rid of it by luck; otherwise, the danger is very great. This year's new tea, except for the black tea from Qimen and Zhide, which had poor output due to excessive rainfall, the green tea from Wuyuan and Xiuning, although there was continuous rain when the tea buds first emerged, once the tea gardens opened, the weather became sunny and warm, and the climate was mild. The tea plants not only received frequent nourishment from the morning dew, but also allowed the mountain households to pick and process them at their leisure. Therefore, the new tea produced is exceptionally tender, the quality is heavier, and the color and flavor are excellent, truly worthy of being called top grade.

Mountain Prices Increase 108

Tea firms depend on the year's business for their livelihood. When mountain households harvest their gardens, they mobilize scouts to search for and buy tea. The tea farmers initially intended that if this year's output was sold at a loss, selling at a high price would mean a double loss of tea price and would inevitably lose money, so they firmly refused to sell. Tea firms, believing that the market was not rising, insisted on agreeing to the limited price before agreeing to trade. After holding out against each other, the mountain households were burdened by economic pressure, and the tea firms, seeing the loss in production, both parties finally agreed to a balanced opening price. The market price was determined by the quality of the tea, with Qimen black tea priced from 120 to 130 yuan per dan to more than 30 yuan, She tea from 90 yuan to more than 50 yuan, Tun tea from 60 yuan to 70 yuan, and Wu tea from 50 yuan to 70 yuan, all increasing by 10 to 20 yuan compared to the past. Although the cost of tea firms has increased and the mountain households have received a higher price, it only compensates for the reduction in output. However, considering the total loss of revenue in various parts of Anhui, it is estimated that the income has decreased by about two million yuan, which is an invisible but significant loss to the rural economy.

Tea Firms Decrease 109

The purpose of tea firms is to try their best to reduce costs and seek to sell at a good price. In terms of reducing costs, the price of mountain tea seems to be in the hands of the tea firms, so there are often disputes over the mountain price when new tea is put on the market. As a result, the tea firms, eager to purchase tea, find it difficult to agree, and eventually the solidarity crumbles, and they rush to increase the price, until it is sold by the box. The market price is entirely controlled by foreign merchants. Therefore, in the tea trade, there is no right to buy or sell to this day. Tea merchants have long wanted to break through this difficult situation, but ultimately, due to the lack of solidarity and the environment as it is, their dreams have not been realized. The failure of the tea industry is largely due to this. This year, the attitude of tea firms, learning from years of losses, is quite calm, unlike the mutual competition of previous years. The market price has been opened in an orderly manner. Occasionally, cautious tea merchants, seeing the gloomy overseas market, purchase less tea to avoid repeating past mistakes. In total, the number of firms in various counties this year has decreased: Qimen has decreased by more than 30 firms compared to the past, Tunxi has decreased by 7, and She County and Wuyuan have each decreased by more than 20. In this extraordinary year, the purpose of tea merchants is mostly to change course according to the wind, and they are unwilling to lightly take risks in the face of the turbulent waves.

Tea Warehouses Contract 110

The business of tea warehouses is similar in nature to that of brokers, except that they can first extend loans to tea firms. Tea firms that accept loans from a certain warehouse must deliver their boxed tea to that warehouse, which negotiates with foreign firms to sell it. The tea price obtained, after deducting the principal and interest of the warehouse loan and the warehouse's expenses, is used to repay the debt. If the tea firm makes tea with its own capital and sells it without losing money, the warehouse's business income will only be profitable and not loss-making. The silk and tea warehouses in various parts of Anhui are all branches of Shanghai warehouses stationed in the local area. The extension or contraction of loans must be carried out under the command of the Shanghai warehouses. In recent years, due to past losses from indiscriminate lending and the tightening of credit, various warehouses have been more cautious in extending loans. The Shanghai warehouses have also discussed regulations to restrict lending. For example, if a tea firm has not repaid its warehouse loan by the end of the year, the warehouse will report it to the trade association at the beginning of the following year, and other warehouses will not accept the firm or extend tea loans to it. After the implementation of this regulation, few tea warehouses have suffered losses. This year, the warehouses stationed in Anhui still follow the old rules and extend loans to tea firms based on whether the firm itself is sound. Each firm can borrow only 30% to 40% of its total capital. Firms with insufficient strength feel the pain of being unable to maneuver freely. Firms that speculate without capital can only sigh and dare not rashly open shop. The decrease in the number of tea firms in various places this year is indeed due to the tightening of credit.

Sales Prices are Dull 111

The boxed tea from foreign firms in Anhui province is mainly sold to countries such as England, America, France, Africa, Russia, and Germany. Retail shops account for only a small proportion. The tea trade depends entirely on the smoothness, stagnation, rise, and fall of sales prices in overseas markets to determine profit or loss. In the past two years, the market prices offered by foreign merchants for Chinese tea have decreased significantly compared to the past. The selling price of Qimen black tea, due to the increase in mountain prices, is only half of the cost. The losses of tea firms in the past two years have been nearly two million yuan. The profits and losses of Wu and Tun green tea are used to make up for each other, and there is no profit. According to the report of the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau, the quantity of tea exported in the first quarter of this year was 72,623.67 metric tons, a decrease of more than 5,000 metric tons compared to 77,769.66 metric tons in the same quarter last year. The initial export of new green tea this year was only 85 tons. Except for a slight increase in England, all other countries have decreased, especially the United States and Russia. The Moroccan green tea market is also unusually quiet. Among them, the soil firms still have more than 8,000 boxes of Chun Mei and Zhen Mei in stock, and the road firms also have 5,000 boxes. The prices of all kinds of tea are declining. Moreover, the French colonies have implemented a double import tax on Chinese tea exported to the colonies from April 1 this year, that is, 50 yuan in Chinese silver must be levied for each dan of tea. Vietnam is also following suit and is considering increasing the import tax rate on Chinese tea. This kind of harsh tax adds another obstacle to the sale of our country's green tea in France. Last week, the first-grade Zhen Mei from Tunxi was opened in Shanghai at a new price of only 130 yuan, a decrease of 20 to 30 yuan compared to the past. The new red tea from Hekou was only opened at 65 to 66 yuan, and the price of Zhen Mei from Suian has recently fallen sharply by 20 yuan. In the future, the sales prices of Qiwu red and green tea will inevitably be difficult to improve compared to last year. Although the sale of tea this year has been changed to the new market scale, which is converted from pounds to catties, there is a slight compensation, but the amount is very small and insufficient to compensate for the discount in the price. It is unknown to what extent the future market situation will change, but based on the current sales of new tea, it is difficult to expect a turn for the better in Anhui province's tea this year. (May 28)

Gu Renfa's False Accusation Case: Li Shuyun and Her Mother Are Innocent. The Re-Marriage Case Was Heard Yesterday, But Gu Still Failed to Appear After Being Summoned. 112

(Wuxi News) The case of Gu Renfa, former Director of the Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department, being accused by Li Shuyun of re-marriage and false accusation has been twice summoned by the local branch court of this county for investigation. Gu has refused to appear. Yesterday (2nd) was another court date for this case. A summons was issued to Gu Renfa, Li Shuyun, and Li Liu before the hearing, but Gu Renfa still failed to appear. Only Li Shuyun and her mother appeared as summoned. At 3:30 PM, Prosecutor Qian of the first instance began the hearing in the investigation court. Li Shuyun and her mother requested that Gu Renfa be arrested and severely punished. If he could not be arrested, they requested an order for his wanted status. The judge approved the request and instructed them to submit a written request for arrest. The court was then adjourned. Regarding the parts of Gu Renfa's false accusation against Li Shuyun and Li Liu of instigating Liu Zhuomin to resist transfer, obstructing official duties, and selling official positions for fraud, the Chief Prosecutor Qian has now completed the investigation and believes that the Li Shuyun and her mother do not have sufficient criminal suspicion. Yesterday, he had already issued a decision not to prosecute. Now, the original text of the decision not to prosecute has been obtained and copied as follows: "Defendant Gu Li Shuyun, 22 years old, from Changsha, Hunan; Li Liu, 50 years old, from Changsha, Hunan; The aforementioned case of instigating obstruction of official duties and fraud, Case No. 776 of the General Letter of 1934, has been fully investigated in accordance with the law. This office believes that a decision not to prosecute should be made. The facts and reasons are now stated below: Gu Li Shuyun is the daughter of Li Liu and the wife of Gu Renfa, the former Director of the Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department. After Gu Renfa became the Director of the Civil Affairs Department, he resided at No. 1 Taigu Mountain, Zhenjiang. Li Liu temporarily stayed at Gu's home to take care of her daughter's illness. On March 12 of this year, Liu Zhuomin, Director of the Second Branch of the Wuxi County Public Security Bureau, was dismissed from his post. Coincidentally, Li Shuyun and her mother, Li Liu, went to Shanghai for medical treatment on the 13th. At the same time, Liu Zhuomin was sent for investigation for obstructing official duties because he hid the seal and refused to hand it over, and his wife, Liu Wen, scolded public officials. Not long after, it was reported that Gu Li Shuyun and Li Liu were suspected of instigating Liu Zhuomin to resist handing over the official seal and were engaged in swindling and deception. In addition, the Wuxi County Government received a telegram from the Jiangsu Provincial Government stating that Li Shuyun and her mother had been arrested by the Civil Affairs Department in Shanghai and were currently detained by the Second Special District Court. It ordered the county to transfer the case to this office for investigation. After repeated inquiries, the defendants Gu Li Shuyun and Li Liu consistently denied instigating Liu Zhuomin to resist handing over the official seal and denied engaging in swindling and deception. The accuser, Gu Renfa, has also repeatedly failed to appear after being summoned. In addition, the Civil Affairs Department has sent various volumes of evidence of Li Shuyun's swindling and deception. After reviewing the volumes of evidence, it is impossible to prove that the defendants committed any crimes. Except for Liu Zhuomin and Liu Wen's obstruction of official duties, which is a separate case, the reasons for the lack of evidence in this case are divided into two points and stated below: (1) The part of instigating obstruction of official duties: To instigate a crime, the criminal act of the person being instigated must be purely the result of the instigator's actions in order to be established. Liu Zhuomin's concealment of the seal was not only denied by Gu Li Shuyun and Li Liu, but Liu Zhuomin also stated in court that he was not instructed by Gu Li Shuyun, etc. It is clear that Liu Zhuomin's obstruction of official duties is unrelated to Gu Li Shuyun. As for the statement that Gu Li Shuyun came to Wuxi on March 13 and met with Liu Zhuomin at the New World Hotel, it was found that Room 60 of the hotel's circulation book was rented by Li Shuyun on that day. It is still questionable whether it was a pseudonym used by Gu Li Shuyun. Even if it is true, it is difficult to use the fact that they met as conclusive evidence of instigating obstruction of official duties. (2) Part of fraud: The original evidence sent was nothing more than the reports of Zeng Fanhong and Hao Ruyuan, and the letters of Zhou Zhengyuan, etc. However, when Zeng Fanhong was questioned in court, he said that when he met Li Fengqi, he asked who was in charge of the Civil Affairs Department that day, what kind of losses Li Fengqi had suffered, and what the amount of the losses was. All of these answers were evasive and could not be answered accurately. Gu Li Shuyun claimed that there was no such person as Li Fengqi in her mother's family, which is sufficient to show that Zeng Fanhong's report is obviously not credible. As for Hao Ruyuan's statement that Li Shuyun called from Nanjing and asked Secretary Wan to maintain Liu Zhuomin's position, it is purely one-sided and difficult to believe. Even if the request was true, it cannot be hastily regarded as fraud. As for Zhou Zhengyuan and others claiming that Li Shuyun sought bribes and sold official positions for money, repeated investigations have yielded no conclusive evidence. In addition, the original evidence sent stated that Gu Shuyun demanded a large sum of money, which was based on the original letter from Huang Jiazhun and the receipt from Gu Li Shuyun. However, according to Li Shuyun's statement, she went to Shanghai for medical treatment on March 13 and stayed at Huang Yiou's house in Xinmin Village. Because of medical expenses, she sent a letter to Gu Renfa asking him to send money and wrote a letter to Secretary Wan Zongzhou. Later, Secretary Wan's surname Huang sent 200 yuan, which was delivered in two installments. The receipts were also given in two installments. There was no borrowing of money from Huang Jiazhun to purchase furniture, etc. When questioned, Huang Jiazhun stated that the 200 yuan was borrowed by Gu Li Shuyun to purchase furniture, etc. However, the receipt presented by Huang Jiazhun had Gu Li Shuyun's business card for the first time and plain paper for the second time, with the words 'Da An came from abroad' and 'Da An sent abroad' on it. Da An is the number of Gu Renfa. It is certain that the money was sent by Gu Renfa when it was delivered, and there is no doubt that it was not borrowed from Huang Jiazhun. Otherwise, Huang Jiazhun would not have accepted this receipt at that time. It is clear that Huang Jiazhun can only be said to have been responsible for the delivery of the money. How can it be forcibly associated with Li Shuyun borrowing and demanding money? As for Li Liu, she only accompanied her daughter Li Shuyun to Shanghai for medical treatment. The facts are very obvious. Even Huang Jiazhun's statement in court did not involve Li Liu at all. Even more so, Li Liu has no crime to speak of. Therefore, in accordance with Articles 244, Paragraphs 2 and 3 of the Criminal Law, a decision not to prosecute is made. Qian Chengyun, Chief Prosecutor of the Wuxi Branch of the Jiangsu Wu County Local Court, May 22, 1934."

Songjiang: Dog Climbs on Roof Extortion Case 113

Xia Ajin, who runs a duck shop in Zhuganhui, has been frugal and has saved a little money, so he has been coveted by bandits. On the 29th of last month, he suddenly received a threatening letter signed by Wang Debiao, which stated that he was short of military pay and that his army protected them, so he needed to borrow 500 yuan. If he refused to borrow, he would send someone to kidnap his nursing son. He was given a deadline to meet at Songhui Xiaozhu. After receiving the letter, Xia did not dare to make a public announcement, but was strictly on guard. Unexpectedly, the previous night, he heard footsteps on the roof. He turned on the light and saw a black foreign-breed pug dog. He drove it away and it jumped down. Because the dog was different from wild dogs, someone must have raised it. How could it climb on the roof? It was obviously related to the threatening letter. He immediately reported the dog and the threatening letter to the Second Branch Police Station, which transferred them to the County Public Security Bureau for investigation. The dog was initially detained in the bureau, and the trail was to be investigated, but accidentally, the dog escaped. It is now being investigated and pursued.

Jiading: Two Daughters Poisoned to Death Case Judgement 114

Chen, the third concubine of Shang Jiaren, the former chairman of the county chamber of commerce, committed suicide by poisoning and at the same time poisoned her two young daughters. She was rescued but did not die. The county government has summoned her three times. Chen did not arrive for the first two summons because she was in Shanghai. At the third court hearing, Chen stated that Gao falsely accused her of having an affair with Qian Xiaofeng, a gatekeeper, and forced her to take poison. She did not know how her two daughters died. Gao admitted to smoking opium and stated that Chen took poison herself and poisoned her two daughters. After reviewing the confession, Judge Shao ruled that Gao and Chen were responsible for the deaths and sentenced them to five years of imprisonment. Gao Jiaren was sentenced to two years of imprisonment for causing death through negligence and fined 300 yuan for smoking opium.

Eighth District Murder Case 115

Chen Ajin, from Changshu Renyang, went to Xu Jingzhai's house in Shuangfeng Town the day before yesterday to collect society fees. While passing through the Fourth Ward of the Sixteenth District of the Eighth District of the county, he was beaten to death by his enemy Yang A'gen and his accomplices Yang Fuxian, Gu A'gen, etc., and his body was thrown into the river. After the incident, Yang, etc. bribed the ward chief with a large sum of money. The ward chief received 70 yuan in bribes and falsely reported the death on the road to the county government. The land inspector also took bribes and went to the countryside to inspect the body. The deceased's family, Chen Shaoyun, etc., feeling aggrieved, reported the incident to the County Public Security Bureau and requested a fair investigation. After the County Bureau received the report, it sent a detective team leader to investigate and found that the report was true. Over the past few days, detectives have been secretly dispatched to arrest the principal offender, Yang A'gen, etc. Yesterday afternoon, a preliminary trial was held. Ward Chief Zhu Ting confessed that the case was handled by Zhao Yangyue, the current commander of the Eighth District Security Regiment, and Zhao Jingyuan, the outgoing district chief. Wang Bao, a patrol officer of the Public Security Bureau, received a bribe of 30 yuan, which was paid by Zhu. The County Bureau, considering that the case involved human life and was complex, sent the witnesses' statements and confessions to the county for legal proceedings.

Suzhou: Garment Industry Continues Strike 116

Garment workers in Suzhou City launched a strike against the Garment Industry Association organized by Chen Yulin, etc. Yesterday (2nd) was the second day. At about 8 a.m., hundreds of workers gathered at the Xuanyuan Public Office in Jiusheng Lane to discuss solutions, but their opinions were divided. The main purpose was to demand the abolition of the Garment Industry Association organized by Chen Yulin, etc., who are not in the industry. In the afternoon, the crowd planned to go to the Public Security Bureau to petition. Director Shen of the Public Security Bureau, fearing that the workers would riot, specially dispatched more police to patrol the Guanqian Street area to maintain law and order. Chen Yulin, the chairman of the Garment Industry Association, who was arrested on the evening of the day before yesterday, is still detained in the Public Security Bureau. After the county government received the Public Security Bureau's report on the strike situation, it has submitted it to the province for review.

Wuxi: Cocoon Industry Control Case Resolved 117

Since the province promulgated the Cocoon Industry Control Regulations, the cocoon industry in this county has unanimously opposed it. There has been a dispute between the government and merchants. Recently, the Cocoon Industry Association of this county has made three requests, asking the authorities to allow flexibility. This was submitted to County Magistrate and Model Sericulture Zone Director Yan Shenyu and Deputy Director Cai Jingde for instructions from the province. The situation has been recorded in this newspaper. It is now known that Yan and Cai returned to Wuxi from the province yesterday. In accordance with the control measures, the spring cocoons of this session are in a hurry, and the procedures may be insufficient. Therefore, special flexibility will be given to the three requests made by the cocoon industry. The request of the first article is approved to open for business, but only for this session. After this, the precedent shall not be cited for handling. The second article, the association voluntarily gives up handling registration procedures and baking worker profits, which is not impossible, but the association shall still be responsible for guaranteeing the guarantee deposit. The third article, the cocoon merchants have already complied with the payment, and the association shall still be responsible for persuading them. Yesterday, a special letter was sent to the Cocoon Industry Association for reference. As of yesterday, there were already 86 cocoon firms reported to be opened in the county. Yesterday, the Model Sericulture Zone of this county also sent personnel to various villages to investigate the cocoon firms.

Changzhou: Cocoon Industry Association Member Meeting 118

In order to prepare for the upcoming listing of fresh cocoons, the Wuyi Cocoon Industry Association convened a member meeting at 2 p.m. on June 1. The following is a list of the key resolutions passed: (1) It is scheduled that all cocoon firms in the county will uniformly open for business on June 6. (2) The cocoon price is stipulated as 25 yuan per dan for improved varieties and 20 yuan for local varieties. (This refers to the old scale. If the new scale is used, it will be calculated according to this discount.) (3) Regarding the improvement fee ordered to be collected at 3 yuan per dan, a representative should be sent to the Ministry of Industry and the Department of Construction to request an exemption from collection.

The section of the road from Jiaxing to Suzhou that was damaged by landslides has now been repaired. In order to expand business, additional bus services have been added starting from June 1, connecting with the train schedules of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou lines to facilitate travel.

Anti-Opium Society's June 3rd Commemoration Declaration 128

"The Chinese Anti-Opium Society, taking today as the 95th anniversary of Lin Zexu's burning of opium at Humen, and at a time when our country's New Life Movement is experiencing a surge from lax to strict opium prohibition, urgently calls upon the people to devote themselves to the anti-opium movement. A commemorative ceremony was held today, and important statements will be made regarding the opium prohibition stance and the future of anti-opium efforts. The declaration of the society is excerpted as follows:

The commemoration of Lin Gong's burning of opium has continued year after year, and the opium scourge has become increasingly rampant. Internal and external troubles have followed, which is truly heartbreaking. Recently, the domestic anti-opium atmosphere has intensified through the advocacy of anti-opium comrades from various quarters. Opium dens in Wuhan were closed first, and Chairman Chiang's decree banning drugs was promulgated later. Anhui, Fujian, and other southeastern provinces have all cleared opium seedlings, which is somewhat satisfactory. However, the transport of raw opium on the Yangtze River has not stopped, and the opium prohibition in various provinces still lacks a definite stance. Inland warlords still rely on opium taxes to maintain their military supplies. The Ping-Liao railway construction request is actually aimed at facilitating the transport of raw opium into the interior. While North China has not yet been lost, Japanese and Korean rogues have intensified their conspiracy to spread drugs, causing fundamental destruction. Recently, Chairman Soong toured the Northwest and deeply felt the ferocity of the opium scourge. Looking around the country, apart from Shandong and Zhejiang, where the results of opium prohibition are somewhat remarkable, there is nothing to say in other provinces. Now that Chairman Chiang has issued strict orders, he will definitely implement his stance. Vice Commander Zhang has returned from studying abroad and also strongly advocates opium prohibition. The legislative and supervisory authorities have protested the opium ban repeatedly, which shows that the authorities are all aware of this, and it is very gratifying. Indeed, in today's situation in our country, we cannot save the nation without resisting Japan, and we cannot survive without banning opium, and banning opium is a prerequisite for resisting Japan. The people's physical strength is weak, their spirits are depressed, and the sick man has even become an opium addict. How can we resist strong enemies and defend the country? Moreover, the New Life Movement is being promoted everywhere, and all levels of society are studying the ancient precepts of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame, and forging new rules of strength, health, and cleanliness. Opium and all narcotics are the chief of all poisons and the source of all filth. Those who indulge in them become withered in body and degenerate in morality. The most humble, weak, and shameless creatures in the world are indeed opium addicts. In recent times, the corruption of officialdom has been lamented as a sign of national demise. Although the reasons vary, the most powerful factors at play are the collection of opium taxes and the trade in narcotics. Therefore, if the drug scourge is not eradicated, the official system cannot be rectified. Which patriotic and sensible person does not sympathize with this statement? Lin Wenzhong Gong said, "If opium is not banned, in ten years, not only will there be no funds to raise, but there will also be no soldiers to use." How painful and accurate are these words! Alas, whose fault is it that China has fallen into ruin? We have nurtured sores and brought about calamity, taking the blame upon ourselves. This society has been fighting against opium for ten years, and what we have seen is clearer, and what we have said is more painful. Previously, we called opium the vanguard of the strong neighbors' aggression, the source of political evil, the source of famine and bandits, and the main cause of the people's distress. Those who did not know thought we were deliberately making alarming statements to sensationalize the public, but now they have all unfortunately been verified. On this day of serious national crisis, we must rise up together and eradicate the source of the disease. This society, upholding the legacy of the Premier and entrusted by the people, will adhere to its past stance and strive to the end. We hereby declare."

Meeting Order 131

(1) Ring the bell to start; (2) Publicly elect a temporary chairman; (3) Bow three times to the Party and National Flag and the Premier's portrait; (4) The chairman respectfully reads the Premier's will; (5) Silence; (6) The chairman reports the number of shareholders present and the total number of shares; (7) Report on the preparatory work; (8) Pass the company's articles of association; (9) Elect the first board of directors and supervisors; (10) The directors and supervisors read the investigation report; (11) Adjourn the meeting.

Meeting Circumstances 132

At 4:45, all the shareholders had gathered one after another. The bell was rung to start the meeting immediately, and the ceremony was performed as usual. Li Shizeng was publicly elected as the temporary chairman, Xie Zuokai was the master of ceremonies, and Yao Yongli recorded the minutes. First, the chairman reported that the number of attendees was 98 people, with a total of 96,700 shares. Then, Yao Yongli, on behalf of the chairman, reported on the preparatory work. Yao then read the articles of association one by one, and the entire meeting amended and passed them. Immediately afterwards, the election of the first board of directors and supervisors was held. Zhang Peishen was elected to count the votes, and Zhou Shouliang called out the votes. As a result, Kong Yongzhi, Song Ziwen, and 19 others were elected as directors, and Zhang Jingjiang, Ye Zhuotang, and 5 others were elected as supervisors. The meeting adjourned at 9 o'clock.

Preparatory Work 133

Attorney Yao Yongli, representing the chairman, reported on the preparatory work, saying that since the establishment of this company, Mr. Kong Yongzhi, Mr. Song Ziwen, Mr. Xie Zuokai, Mr. Zhang Jingjiang, Mr. Li Shizeng, and other leaders of the national financial and economic circles have seen the stagnation of domestic industry, commerce, and various enterprises and are urgently seeking ways to remedy the situation. They believe that unless domestic capital is pooled, domestic enterprises and industry and commerce are supported, and guidance and supervision are given, there is no way to survive. Therefore, at the end of last year, they initiated the organization of this company. It was not until April 18 that the share-raising articles of association and other documents were submitted to the Bureau of Social Affairs for record and submitted to the Ministry of Finance for approval. On April 24, the Bureau of Social Affairs issued an order approving the record. On May 28, the Ministry of Finance issued an order approving the approval. It has been found that the company's authorized capital is 10 million yuan, all of which has been raised by the Chinese people and has now been fully paid up and deposited in various domestic banks. According to the law, a founding general meeting should be convened immediately. Therefore, at noon on May 31, a meeting of initiators was convened at the temporary office of the company on the sixth floor of the Continental Bank on Jiujiang Road, and the Bureau of Social Affairs was requested to send personnel to attend the founding meeting for supervision. The above is the preparatory work of this company. Please ask the shareholders to discuss the articles of association one by one, etc.
