Articles of Association Passed 135

The original text of the articles of association is as follows: Articles of Association of China Construction Bank Co., Ltd. Chapter 1 General Provisions. Article 1: This company is organized in accordance with the provisions of the Company Law, the current laws and regulations of joint-stock companies and banks, and is named China Construction Bank Co., Ltd., abbreviated as China Construction Bank. The English name is (The Ghina Deyclopmenl Finance Coeooration). Article 2: The head office of this company is located at No. 111 Jiujiang Road, Shanghai. This company may establish branches in various places at home and abroad, but it shall first be resolved by the board of directors, submitted to the Ministry of Finance for approval and registration, and submitted to the Ministry of Industry for registration. Article 3: The business term of this company is 30 years, calculated from the date of registration with the Department of Industry. Upon expiration, it may be extended with the resolution of the shareholders' meeting and the approval of the Ministry of Finance and the Department of Industry. Article 4: The method of announcement of this company shall be by circular and published in famous newspapers in the location of the head office. Chapter 2 Shares. Article 5: The total capital of this company is fixed at 10 million yuan in national currency, divided into 1 million shares, each share is 10 yuan in national currency, and is paid up at one time. When this company needs to increase capital and issue new shares due to business needs, it shall be resolved by the shareholders' meeting and issued after being submitted to the Ministry of Finance for registration and the Department of Industry for registration in accordance with the law. If preferred shares are issued, all rights that preferred shares should have shall be added to the articles of association by resolution of the shareholders' meeting before issuance and submitted to the Ministry of Finance and the Department of Industry for approval and record. Article 6: The shares of this company shall be signed, sealed, numbered, and issued by five directors of this company after being approved for registration. Article 7: The shareholders of this company shall be registered, and shall report their true names and addresses and those of their representatives to this company and record them in the shareholders' register. The same shall apply to any changes. Article 8: Shareholders shall fill in the seal on the seal form and submit it to this company for safekeeping for verification. All receipts of dividends, bonuses, and written matters useful to this company shall be based on this seal. Article 9: The procedures for changing the name, transferring, analyzing, merging, losing, damaging, or otherwise disposing of the shares of this company and changing the seal shall be specified in separate rules. Article 10: The transfer of shares shall be suspended from the date of notification of the shareholders' meeting to the date of completion of the shareholders' meeting. Chapter 3 Business. Article 11: The scope of business of this company shall be to assist and jointly with government agencies, Chinese and foreign banks, and other organizations to support various types of public and private enterprises, develop agriculture, industry, and commerce, and handle investment and management affairs related to these businesses and all affairs of trust companies. The method, method, and procedure to be adopted for the foregoing business shall be resolved by the board of directors of this company at any time and submitted to the Ministry of Finance for approval and record. The trust business within the scope of the foregoing business shall establish a special department, allocate capital by resolution of the shareholders' meeting, formulate separate articles of association, and submit them to the Ministry of Finance and the Department of Industry for approval and record. Chapter 4 Shareholders' Meeting. Article 12: The shareholders' meeting of this company is divided into two types: regular meetings and temporary meetings. (1) The regular meeting shall be convened by the board of directors one month in advance within three months after the final annual accounts. (2) A temporary meeting shall be convened by the board of directors 15 days in advance when the board of directors or the supervisors deem it necessary, or when requested by the shareholders of this company in accordance with the provisions of Article 133 of the Company Law. Article 13: The right to vote and the right to vote of the shareholders of this company shall be one right for each share, but a shareholder who has more than 11 shares shall have nine rights for every ten shares exceeding ten shares, and the remainder shall not be counted. Article 14: The shareholders' meeting must have shareholders holding more than one-half of the total number of shares of this company to be convened, and a resolution may be passed with the consent of more than one-half of the voting rights present. However, when changing the articles of association and increasing or decreasing capital, it shall be carried out in accordance with the provisions of Article 186 of the current Company Law. Article 15: The convocation of the shareholders' meeting shall be announced in the newspaper or notified to the shareholders by letter, stating the date, location, purpose of convocation, and agenda. Article 16: If shareholders have proposals, they shall submit them to the board of directors for review five days before the opening of the meeting and include them in the agenda. Article 17: Shareholders may entrust other shareholders of this company to represent them at the shareholders' meeting, but they shall submit a power of attorney to this company. Article 18: The matters of the shareholders' meeting shall be recorded in the resolution minutes, including the date, time, location, name of the chairman, number of shareholders present, total number of shares, and the matters discussed. The chairman shall sign and seal the minutes and keep them together with the attendance book and the power of attorney for representation in this company. Chapter 5 Organization. Article 19: This company shall have 21 directors and 7 supervisors, who shall be elected by the shareholders' meeting from the shareholders holding more than 1,000 shares. Article 20: The term of office of directors is three years, and the term of office of supervisors is one year, and both may be re-elected. Article 21: The directors shall elect one person as the chairman of the board of directors, and ten persons shall be elected as standing directors. The chairman of the board is the ex officio standing director. The chairman of the board is the chairman of the board of directors, the standing committee of the board of directors, and the shareholders' meeting. If the chairman of the board is unable to attend due to an accident, the board of directors shall elect one person from among the directors as the chairman. Article 22: This company shall appoint three executive directors. In addition to the chairman of the board of directors being the ex officio executive director, the remaining two persons shall be elected by the standing directors. Article 23: The executive directors shall be stationed in this company on a regular basis and supervise all affairs of this company in accordance with the resolutions of the board of directors and the standing committee of the board of directors. Article 24: The board of directors' meeting shall be convened by the chairman of the board of directors. A quorum shall be present if more than one-half of the directors are present, and a resolution may be passed with the consent of more than one-half of the directors present. In case of a tie, the chairman shall decide. If the chairman of the board of directors is unable to convene the board of directors' meeting due to an accident, the standing committee of the board of directors may convene it. The minutes of the board of directors' meeting shall be signed and sealed by each director present and kept in this company. The director concerned shall not have the right to vote on a proposal concerning himself. The detailed rules of the standing committee of the board of directors shall be formulated separately. Article 25: The supervisors shall review the various accounts sent by the board of directors to the shareholders' meeting and report their opinions to the shareholders' meeting. Article 26: The supervisors may request the board of directors to report on the business situation of this company and inspect the various accounts and documents of this company at any time. Article 27: If the directors and supervisors are short of the quota due to an accident, the person with the most votes in the election of the current term shall be appointed to fill the vacancy in turn, and their term of office shall be limited to the term of office of the predecessor. Article 28: This company shall have one general manager, who shall be appointed by the board of directors. If the general manager is unable to perform his duties due to an accident, one person may be elected by the standing directors to act on his behalf. Article 29: The general manager shall implement the resolutions of the board of directors and the standing committee of the board of directors and handle the affairs of this company in consultation with the executive directors. Article 30: This company may appoint managers, deputy managers, and assistant managers depending on the complexity of the affairs. The number and candidates shall be proposed by the general manager and approved by the board of directors for use. Article 31: Other employees of this company shall be appointed by the general manager in consultation with the executive directors. Chapter 6 Final Accounts. Article 32: This company shall make a final account once every six months and a final account at the end of the year. The following forms shall be made:

Page 13

Register with the supervisors three days before the shareholders' meeting, check, seal, and submit to the shareholders' meeting for approval, announce according to law, and submit to the Ministry of Finance and the Department of Industry for verification and record. (1) Business report; (2) Inventory of assets; (2) Balance sheet; (4) Profit and loss statement (3) Public reserve fund and surplus interest distribution plan. Article 33: At least one-tenth of the annual net profit shall be set aside as a public reserve fund, and then dividends shall be distributed. Article 34: The annual interest rate is seven percent. Article 35: After deducting the public reserve fund and paying dividends from the net profit, if there is still a surplus, it shall be used as shareholders' bonuses and employees' rewards, and a special public reserve fund may be appropriated as appropriate. The distribution method shall be submitted by the board of directors to the shareholders' meeting for resolution and reported to the Ministry of Finance for record, but the employees' rewards shall not exceed 30% of the surplus profit of the year. Chapter 7 Supplementary Provisions. Article 36: The various rules of procedure of this company shall be formulated by the board of directors. Article 37: Matters not covered in these articles of association shall be handled in accordance with the provisions of the Company Law and the current laws and regulations of banks. Article 38: These articles of association shall be implemented from the date of approval, registration, and filing with the Ministry of Finance and the Department of Industry. If there are any changes to be made in the future, they shall be resolved by the shareholders' meeting in accordance with the law and submitted for approval and filing.

Exceptional Interpretation of Trademark Law; Machine Industry Association Requests Supplementation 136

The Joint Association of Machinery-Made Domestic Goods Factories in this city sent a letter to Jiao Yitang, Chairman of the Legislative Yuan's Legal System Committee, and all members yesterday regarding the Trademark Law, stating: "Respectfully, this association previously submitted a document to the Legislative Yuan on April 16 of this year, stating that the interpretation of the Trademark Law is exceptional and hinders national confidence, and requesting that a proposal be made to supplement it. According to Article 1, Paragraph 2 of the Trademark Law, the words, graphics, and symbols are originally three types. If the words do not contain sound and meaning, they are no different from graphics and symbols. Why must words be the prerequisite? This shows that words must contain sound and meaning. The difference between a person who can read and a person who cannot read lies in whether or not they can pronounce the word. If a deaf person wants to test whether they know this word or not, they must write another word with the same sound to show to others. This is a matter of course. However, when people who cannot read buy and sell goods, it depends entirely on what they hear and say. If trademarks with different words but the same sound are allowed to be registered, wouldn't this

Encourage Confusion? 137

Therefore, this is not allowed by the Trademark Bureau's usual practice. However, since the Executive Yuan requested the Judicial Yuan to interpret it, it has been said that words do not contain sound and meaning and are treated as graphics and symbols in general, which will allow tricksters to compete to use trademarks with different words but the same sound to deceive the public, affect the future of industry and commerce, and overturn the precedents of the Trademark Law. The dignity of trademark registration has fundamentally disappeared. Whether internal or external, it is enough to hinder national confidence. The only way to do this now is to request your esteemed Yuan to supplement Articles 1 and 2 of the Trademark Law in the spirit of legislation, so as to reassure people and prevent the trend of trickery. Judging from the original meaning of Article 1, Paragraph 2, it is very broad and does not necessarily need to specify that words include sound and meaning. Because no one else has registered before, there is no such thing as similarity. Therefore, its crackdown is listed in the various clauses of Article, which is very appropriate in the original intention of legislation. However, regarding "designated colors," it is proposed to add a "得" (dé, can) character under the "并" (bìng, and) character, because according to the original regulations, only one color is clearly used, or there is no color at all, such as those used on glass bottles and iron boxes. However, those who imitate can argue by taking different colors. If the original registrant has to prevent its drawbacks, first register all the similar trademarks of various colors one by one. The Trademark Bureau can get a large income, but the industrial and commercial households cannot afford it, and it is

Impossible to Prevent 138

Therefore, if a "得" (dé, can) character is added, those that are not necessary but similar are already in the list of natural crackdowns. This is the request for Article 1, Paragraph 2. After listing the various clauses in Article 2, it is proposed to add a clause saying, "The similarity or approximation mentioned in the preceding paragraph includes the shape, color, sound, and meaning of words, graphics, and symbols. All those who have the suspicion of suggestion are included in it." Because the Trademark Law has no clear regulations on the definition of similarity, it is a major shortcoming. As a result, the same case has different results and contradicts each other, making people at a loss. Now that it has been clearly stipulated, it is enough to prevent trickery and avoid various disputes. For this reason, I am submitting this document to your esteemed Yuan for consideration, so as to contribute a fool's opinion. I am looking forward to it very much. After the presentation was made, on May 21, a letter was received from the Secretariat of the Legislative Yuan, which opened, "A document was issued by the President of the Yuan, 'The interpretation of the Trademark Law is exceptional,

Hindering National Confidence, 139

Please supplement Articles 1 and 2 of the law and consider it.' It was approved to be handed over to the Commercial Law Committee for record." In addition to handing it over as directed, I am corresponding to inform you that I have seen the intention of your esteemed Yuan to care for the people's concerns and sympathize with the difficulties of businesses. Not only are the 286 member factories of our association leading and hoping, but all those who read the newspaper are like seeing clouds and rain. However, for the past month, there has been no impact, and counterfeit and suggestive trademarks have sprung up like bamboo shoots after rain and flooded the market. Since they cannot be brought to justice, how can the hearts of good people be comforted? For this reason, I venture to submit this official letter, requesting that your seat take the spirit of legislation as the basis and quickly check the original submission, propose a supplement, so as to prevent tricksters from taking advantage of the loopholes and exempt those who always worry about their business. The matter is related to trademark credibility, which is observed by Chinese and foreign people. I hope that you will find a way to remedy it and ensure national credibility. It is a great blessing. Sincerely submitted to the Chairman and Members of the Legal System Committee of the Legislative Yuan, The Joint Association of Machinery-Made Domestic Goods Factories."

Provisional General Meeting of the Shipping Guild Discusses the Detention of the Jing'an Vessel; Resolution to Petition for the Establishment of a Provisional Arbitration Tribunal for Special Adjudication 141

The Shanghai Shipping Industry Guild, regarding the detention of the Sanbei Company's Jing'an steamship, convened a provisional general membership meeting on the afternoon of May 31st, following a resolution by the executive committee. Fifty members attended. Chairman Yuan Lvdeng reported the purpose of the meeting, stating that the provisional general membership meeting was convened based on the executive committee's resolution due to the wrongful detention of the Sanbei Company's Jing'an steamship. Of the eighty members of the guild, fifty members and representatives were present, constituting a quorum. The meeting should commence immediately, and Mr. Yu Qiaqing of the Sanbei Company was requested to report on the details of the case.

Yu Qiaqing reported that in January of this year, a Fuzhou small steamship sank off Longju Sandbar. The shipowner, Yu Shicheng, falsely accused the Sanbei Company's Jing'an steamship of causing the sinking and filed a lawsuit with the Shanghai District Court. The court, based on a one-sided accusation, and without conducting an inspection, hastily issued a letter to the Jianghai Customs Superintendent's Office, which forwarded the letter to detain the ship. The Customs Superintendent, without investigating the circumstances, followed the court's letter and detained the ship. Subsequently, they were ordered to provide a guarantee of 80,000 yuan before the ship could be released. The detention has lasted nearly fifty days.

Upon investigation, the Zhenjiang authorities verified the Jing'an steamship's logbook, proving the time of arrival in Zhenjiang. Furthermore, the Shanghai Maritime Administration's Ship Collision Dispute Resolution Committee conducted an investigation and determined that the sinking was not caused by the Jing'an steamship. The plaintiff initially claimed that the red paint under the anchor chain hole on the starboard side of the Jing'an steamship was scraped, indicating a collision. However, the paint under the anchor chain hole of a steamship is easily damaged due to friction from the frequent raising and lowering of the anchor. This point was determined by the Ship Collision Dispute Resolution Committee as not being evidence of a collision. The plaintiff then claimed that the dents on the ship's hull were evidence of a collision. However, the dents on the Jing'an steamship's hull were seven feet below the waterline. The ship was carrying 1,500 tons of cargo on that day, with a draft of fourteen feet, making it highly unlikely that the dents were caused by a collision.

The Ministry of the Navy, regarding the detention of the Jing'an, requested the Ministry of Justice to order its release, stating that ship collisions are common occurrences. In the event of an accident, the port authorities should investigate witnesses and examine documentary and physical evidence upon arrival at the port for use in litigation. There is no precedent for indefinitely detaining a seagoing vessel involved in transportation and commerce. Moreover, the owner of the Jing'an, the Shanghai Sanbei Company, is subject to litigation. If a judgment is made requiring compensation, the company would naturally bear that responsibility. Maritime regulations regarding liability pertain to the owner, which is the common practice in all countries. While the litigation procedures of our courts do not necessarily have to be the same as those of other countries, the method of enforcement should not be uniquely different. Maritime transportation is related to maritime affairs, and at a time when international shipping routes are developing, international practices should be taken into consideration. Courts cannot detain ships in cases of ship collisions, and the explanation is very clear.

However, the Shanghai District Court disregarded everything and prolonged the detention, demanding a guarantee. If this precedent is set, the future of the shipping industry is unimaginable. Moreover, at a time when the nation is united in advocating for the recovery of shipping rights and the abolition of extraterritoriality, the impact is even greater. Although the Sanbei Company can勉力 manage to raise 80,000 yuan in cash with great difficulty, other smaller companies would face losses of 30,000 to 40,000 yuan after a month of detention and would be required to provide a guarantee of 80,000 yuan. Regardless of the outcome of the litigation, the company would already be bankrupt. Therefore, for the sake of the shipping industry's future, even if there is sufficient cash to provide a guarantee, it is inappropriate to rashly set this precedent and become the罪人 of the shipping industry. Although the detention of the Jing'an is a sacrifice for the Sanbei Company alone, it is of great importance to the future of all shipping merchants. I sincerely present a detailed report of the case and hope that the company will discuss relief measures to rectify the injustice. The Sanbei Company will be grateful, and the industry will be fortunate.

The meeting resolved to send telegrams to the Executive Yuan, the Judicial Yuan, the Ministry of Transportation, the Ministry of Justice, and the Ministry of the Navy, requesting that a provisional arbitration tribunal be specially established to adjudicate the case fairly and provide relief before a maritime arbitration organization is established. Regarding the Ministry of Transportation's formulation of a table of the number of crew members on ships and the deadline for crew certification, the resolution was to send a telegram to the Ministry of Transportation to examine the actual difficulties. For coastal and river ships, if it is temporarily impossible to replace all crew members with those holding appropriate certificates, crew members holding lower-level certificates should be temporarily allowed to act as substitutes to avoid suspension of navigation.

Subsequently, Member Wang Bolao proposed to discuss the shipping cooperation plan. Member Yang Guanbei seconded the proposal. After the chairman consulted the opinions of the members, they unanimously approved it. Secretary-General Chen was designated to report on the process. Chairman Chen then requested a public discussion. Committee Member Chen Ganqing suggested that shipping cooperation is an essential plan to save ourselves from danger and should be actively promoted to achieve realization. However, it is crucial to clarify whether each company agrees to cooperate in order to facilitate statistics. A letter should be sent to each member asking whether they agree to effective cooperation, and a reply should be requested within two weeks of receiving the letter. It would be even more desirable if the cooperation methods could be disclosed together. The resolution was passed according to the original proposal.

Industry Regulations Passed 144

The articles of association for the rice group's implementation of industry regulations include: general principles, objectives, members and staff, guarantees for each trade, guarantee savings funds, business area meetings, the rights and obligations of members, disciplinary actions and rewards, and supplementary provisions, totaling eleven chapters and twenty-four articles. The following are excerpts of some of the important articles:

Chapter Seven, Article Nine (Business Area): The area south of the 16th Pier and within the city walls is the Southern District. The area north of the 16th Pier to the Wusong River, Xizang Road, Mintiniyin Road, and Nanyang Bridge is the Central District. The area west of Xizang Road and Nanyang Bridge to Caojiadu and Xujiahui is the Western District. The area north of the Suzhou River and west of North Sichuan Road is the Northern District. Chapter Ten, Article Thirty (Disciplinary Actions and Rewards): If a member violates the provisions of Articles Twelve (1) and (2) of the chapter of this subgroup, after a member reports it and the district group leader verifies the facts, the report shall be submitted to the general group leader for the following disciplinary actions: (1) For the first violation of the articles of association, a merchant shall be fined 50 yuan, and a member shall be fined 10 yuan. For the second violation of the articles of association, the penalty shall be doubled. For the third violation of the articles of association, the penalty shall be added to the second penalty. After the above fines are decided upon, they shall be paid to the guild within five days and shall not be deliberately delayed. If the payment is overdue, the amount to be fined shall be deducted from the certificate deposit. (2) Those who have committed three violations and do not repent and dare to violate the articles of association again are intentionally disrupting industry regulations and hindering the public interest of the industry. It is difficult to tolerate them. The merchant shall be reported to the guild for revocation of the measure, and the member shall have their certificate and badge revoked, their membership canceled, and they shall never be allowed to join the guild again.

Chapter Eleven, Article Twenty (Supplementary Provisions): The commission rebate set and implemented by the guild is currently 6 cents per stone for immediate returns and 3 cents per stone for monthly returns. Overdue payments will not be refunded.

Kong Xiangrong Discusses the Closure Project: The Function of Building Water Sluice Dams 147

According to the Central News Agency, Kong Xiangrong, director of the work relief group of the Yellow River Flood Relief Committee, discussed the impeachment by Supervisory Commissioner Shao Hongji, saying that the three impeachments by Supervisory Commissioner Shao were for Kong's proposition of building a closed-air dam with water sluice dams at the kiln head. This matter has been brewing for a long time. Previously, it was heard that the third impeachment had been reviewed and rejected. Now, seeing the newspaper report that it has been passed and handed over to the Disciplinary Committee, the reason for its passage is not understood.

The method used by the previous administration to close the breach at Fenglou was a water-permeable stone dam. Although Rong quickly completed the closing of the breach in a very short time, the flow continued due to water permeability. Adding a water sluice dam behind the stone dam has three advantages: (1) It can consolidate the front stone dam and gain water resistance; (2) It can cut off the flow after the dam is closed, preventing the newly built embankment at Shitou Village from becoming dangerous; and (3) It can prevent the people of dozens of villages between the stone dam and Shitou Village from being flooded again.

Since the water level rose in late April, the stone dam has remained permeable, so the water level in front of the kiln head water dam has increased. Because the water dam has been closed, the water level behind the dam is lower, with a difference of more than seven市尺 between the front and back. This is clear evidence that the stone dam is permeable and the water dam cuts off the flow. Without this water dam as a barrier, the top of the new embankment at Shitou Village would be level with the water, posing a dangerous threat. Moreover, the project to raise and thicken the new embankment cannot obtain soil from the river.

The nature of the Yellow River is changeable. Those in charge believe that no work needs to be done when the water is low, but they are panicked and do not know how to defend when the water rises. This is because the nature of the river is different, the responsibilities are different, so the vision is different, and the propositions are also different. Because he is unwilling to agree with others, there have been these three impeachments. However, this dam project has been approved and filed, and Chairman Li of the Yellow River Conservancy Commission has certified that it is a foolproof plan. The three financial directors of Hebei, Shandong, and Henan, dispatched by the committee, and Zhang, committee member and secretary-general of the Yellow River Conservancy Commission, inspected the results and believed that it was necessary to build this water dam. After submitting the report to the committee, they received a telegram ordering them to rush to build it and immediately close it. Various local groups along the river visited the construction site and submitted a petition requesting special protection for the water dam to ensure its permanent protection. The committee has telegraphed the Hebei Provincial Government, which has replied that it has ordered the River Affairs Bureau to comply. The effectiveness of this dam is very obvious, and it is clear that it is not a waste of public funds. If the impeachment is established, all important letters and telegrams will be reviewed and reported again.

However, this water dam has been effective at low water levels and will be even more effective during the peak flood season. To carry out construction work in this changeable Yellow River, preparations with a longer-term vision are necessary to achieve temporary defense effects. How dare we not be careful? Rong only seeks to fulfill his duties and does not care about other things.

Zhenru District New Life Movement Propaganda Meeting 148

Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, the Zhenru District New Life Movement Preparatory Committee held a propaganda meeting at the Sixth Simple Sports Field. Over 2,000 people from various groups and the public attended. After performing the礼行, Chairman Chen Zhongfu reported, saying that the New Life Movement is not a profound theory. It is to teach people how to be human, the purpose and goals, and the methods to implement it. All human behaviors and thoughts that adopt the New Life Movement are the best people in the world. He then explained the four words of礼义　耻 in detail and hoped that we must at least achieve the two points of neatness and cleanliness. Subsequently, Committee Member Hong, Section Chief Zhou, Xu Yizhou, Song Erte, and Yang Zhulai gave speeches on stage, full of warnings. After the speeches, the New Life Movement song was sung, and the New Life Covenant was distributed before the meeting was adjourned. It was also heard that there would be a grand提 meeting that evening.

New Drug Industry Requests Separate Regulations for Selling Medical Anesthetics; Requests the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to Forward a Letter to Chairman Chiang 149

The New Drug Guild requested the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to forward a letter to Chairman Chiang, stating, "To request the promulgation of separate regulations for the sale of medical anesthetics in order to facilitate medical treatment and prevent abuses. It is well known that drugs such as morphine, cocaine, and heroin are potent and toxic to society. Chairman Chiang is concerned about this and resolutely promulgated the Strict Prohibition of Potent Narcotics Regulations, with the transport and sale of these drugs punishable by death. This demonstrates the spirit of diligent governance and stopping killing with killing, which moves all people with blood and spirit. However, while the abuse of these toxic drugs is more than enough to destroy the nation and exterminate the race, they are indispensable in modern medical treatment. Western countries have regulations for the sale of these drugs. Even the Chinese Pharmacopoeia promulgated by the former Ministry of Health has detailed records of the properties, uses, and dosages of these toxic drugs, and there are special regulations for their application by licensed physicians and pharmacists. This is because these drugs are essential for treatment and should not be abandoned because of fear of choking. Since the Qing Dynasty strictly prohibited opium, these toxic drugs have also been strictly prohibited at the same time. At that time, modern medicine had not yet emerged, so there was not much hindrance to scientific application. In recent decades, modern medicine has become more and more common, and hospitals and medical schools have been established one after another. The scientific application of these toxic drugs has also become more and more widespread.

We, as merchants engaged in the sale of medical drugs, and various health agencies and licensed physicians, cannot avoid needing these toxic drugs. Refusing them is not allowed by the facts, and complying with them is suspected of violating the law. In desperation, we can only rely on the signature of a licensed physician and then request foreign merchants to supply them. This has become a customary practice but is not in accordance with the law. Although the Ordinance on the Management of Narcotics was promulgated by the municipal government on September 11, 1929, and amended by the municipal government on November 7, 1931, Article 3 states that the import and distribution of narcotics shall be the responsibility of the general management agency designated by the Ministry of the Interior. Later, the Department of Health approved on September 7, 1932, that the Nanjing Central Hospital had been approved by the Executive Yuan to handle this general management agency. After several years, the general management agency has not been established. Therefore, although the Ordinance on the Management of Narcotics has been promulgated, it has not been implemented fundamentally. We have repeatedly asked Director Liu to formulate measures as soon as possible, but there has been no result. We merchants have the intention to abide by the law but have no basis for it and are in a state of embarrassment.

Now, Chairman Chiang deeply hates the poison of addiction and is saving the lives of the people. Strict laws and harsh penalties are rectifying the source. We merchants are all citizens and cannot but be inspired to abide by the law and live up to his expectations. However, the Ordinance on the Management of Narcotics promulgated by the National Government is difficult to implement, and Chairman Chiang has not had time to stipulate the difference between medical use and abuse. Although Article 14 states that matters not provided for in this ordinance shall be governed by other laws, there is actually no basis in fact. We merchants are concerned about our business and cannot avoid the suffering of being caught in a trap. After repeated deliberations, we all believe that legitimate pharmacies should be protected to avoid misunderstandings. We dare to present the following request: to promulgate separate regulations for the sale of medical anesthetics in order to facilitate medical treatment and prevent abuses. Before the above regulations are promulgated and implemented, we also request that the military police and local health agencies be ordered to strictly investigate and differentiate them, so that the use of medical treatment is not abolished in the strict prohibition of potent narcotics, and they do not conflict with each other. The health of the people will be increased, and not only will the medical community benefit greatly in their duties, but also those who are suffering from diseases will receive painless relief. The scientific future of the medical business relies on this. We sincerely present our request for your consideration.

Jianghai Customs Proclamation Exempts Hainan Rubber Export Tax; Limited to Rubber and Raw Rubber 151

The Jianghai Customs issued Proclamation No. 1365 yesterday, regarding the exemption of export and transit taxes on rubber produced in Guangdong and Hainan, as ordered by the Ministry of Finance's Customs Administration. The proclamation stated that export taxes on rubber produced in Guangdong and Hainan when transported overseas and transit taxes on rubber when sold domestically are exempt across the board. From May 26th of this year, when rubber produced in Hainan is transported to foreign countries or domestic trading ports, export taxes or transit taxes should be exempted separately. However, this tax-exempt item refers specifically to raw rubber or raw rubber, not processed rubber. All merchants are notified.

The land ownership is concerned, so do not delay.

Dane Dangerously Crosses to Japan in a Fast Boat; Departs from Customs Wharf One Day; Scheduled to Arrive in Nagasaki on the Sixth 154

Yesterday, the Japanese-language Mainichi Shimbun reported that a Danish man, Colonel S.D. Georgiensen, a member of the Shanghai Leading River Concession, had designed and built a small speedboat, the "Danaskotte," at the end of last year. He departed from the Customs Wharf at 6:00 PM on the first of the month, preparing to cross the East China Sea to Nagasaki. He was accompanied by N.D. Fujisheng, an employee of the Wante Company, and one Chinese boatman, for a total of three people. The boat has two masts, is 27 feet long and 9 feet wide, and has a total tonnage of 2.5 tons. It was built in Shanghai at the end of last year with joint funding from a Scottish friend. The name of the boat is a combination of the names of Denmark and Scotland. The front of the boat has a cabin painted green that can accommodate two people. The stern is a semi-cruiser type. The hull is all white. The rigging is modeled after Chinese sails. The boat is equipped with a 24-horsepower engine, and its speed is 4-5 knots. The T-type Ford style.

There have been four previous attempts to cross from Shanghai to Nagasaki by speedboat (the "Curlew" and "Nidaros" in 1931, 1932, and 1933). The previous crossings took six days. This time, the voyage is still scheduled to follow the same route, stopping at Wusong for one day and night, departing for Japan on the morning of the second, and planning to tour the Japanese coast depending on the conditions upon arrival, returning to Shanghai around the end of this month. However, according to Japanese reports, the sea route is known as a "devil's sea" and is often plagued by sharks (man-eating fish), but Georgiensen paid no attention to it.

A person from Qingkou named Song Debiao acted suspiciously. Five packages of red pills, each containing 495 pills, were found under his seat. The National Goods Movement Exhibition in Penglai Market, sponsored by the China National Products Manufacturers Association, was the second day of its opening yesterday. It opened at 9:00 AM and closed at 10:00 PM. More than 50,000 people visited, and the business of major manufacturers exceeded the records of previous sessions. The grand occasion is recorded as follows:

Various Circles Visited

The exhibition opened at 9:00 AM, and by 10:00 AM it was already crowded with people. Among the guests who visited were representatives from various trade associations, including Zhu Gengtao of the cotton textile industry, Wu Hanliang and Li Ruzhang of the antique guild, and Ying Yongfeng of the Chinese Dental Protection Association. In addition, the total number of visitors reached more than 50,000, which can be described as a grand occasion.

Business Records

The association has a statistics office for daily business, and all participating manufacturers report their business numbers after closing each day for registration and statistics, which are announced daily. The total business volume for the previous two days reached more than 100,000 yuan, breaking the new business record of previous exhibitions, which is a good manifestation of the national spirit of using domestic goods.

The association, in order to participate in the Shanghai Municipal Welcome Panchen Blessing Conference, issued a special notice to all manufacturers, unanimously sending representatives to the municipal government to participate in the blessing ceremony. In addition to preparing a car for direct delivery, a corresponding notice is hereby given, hoping that you will participate to support the grand event."

Entertainment and Performances

In order to add to the interest of guests from all walks of life, the association has set up an entertainment venue. Anyone who purchases goods from various manufacturers for more than one silver dollar will receive an entertainment ticket. Customers get cheap and high-quality goods, and watch good and noble entertainment. Yesterday's entertainment included (1) Great Teaching Song, (2) Zheng Yuanhe, (3) Staying Happy, (4) Comic plays, and more than a dozen other kinds, so that the venue was full of people, with almost no room to stand.

Setting Up Fire Protection

In order to protect the safety of manufacturers' business, in addition to the China Safety Chemical Industry Society setting up fire extinguishing liquid, Zhen Dan Factory also sent multiple fire extinguishers, which were installed around the venue, and dispatched personnel to take charge of them, in order to protect the safety of various manufacturers, so that everyone can live and work in peace. A rescue team was also set up to prevent the occurrence of epidemics and measles.

Wang Yuanyi, Chen Chief, and Chief Secretary Li Ping greeted them into their seats, and they were served with fragrant tea and snacks. Then, the clerks Ren Qiwen and Xu Chenghuang, etc., ordered the Ding servants to first move the drugs to the representative's seat one by one to verify the seal and weigh them, and stack them in the venue for burning. Then, various gambling equipment were burned. This time, the burned drugs included 15 pounds of opium, 32 taels and 4 qian, and 58 small packets, 22 and a half pounds of morphine, 3 taels, and 131 small packets, 8 pounds of heroin, 12 packets, 80,290 red pills, 11 pounds, 321 packets, 1,477 sets of smoking utensils, 6 and a half bottles of opium paste, 5 taels, 48 small boxes, 24 morphine needles, 760 opium bubbles, and various other utensils. The gambling equipment included 110 flower club papers, 11 flower club books, 1 mahjong set, 36 domino sets, 22 poker sets, 191 dice, 1 treasure box, 1 lotto (Russian name) gambling equipment, and other miscellaneous items. The burning was completed at around 5:00 PM, and the representatives dispersed.

A Record of Visiting the Shen Brothers' Calligraphy and Painting Exhibition 176

Shen Yinmo and Shen Maishi exhibited their recent works at the Lake Society. Yesterday was the first day. The reporter went to visit. The walls were full of exhibits. Yinmo's calligraphy included a scroll of Leisurely Living, a middle hall of Vow Documents, a book of Stupa Temple inscriptions, various epitaph rubbings, and couplets of regular, running, cursive, and cursive scripts. The legal system was strict, the skeleton was majestic and strong, and it was upright and unpretentious, and the roundness was like a ring. It has the aura of a dragon flying and a tiger jumping, which is far from what historical figures can reach. Maishi's paintings imitated ancient scenery, and all were exquisite, such as imitating Juran Yellow Crane and writing landscape albums, Lushan, Wuyi, Fuchun River, Emei, and other paintings. The brushwork was capable of lifting a tripod, and still had a graceful and neat charm. The gods and reasons were combined, and vulgarity was completely deleted. Finger painting came from skillful hands, especially full of nature. In addition, the fan faces co-operated by the two Shen brothers were linked together like pearls, and there were many fine structures. In short, everything made by people can not follow vulgarity, not cling to the old, and not aim to be strange and different. The uprightness contains changes, and the majesty shows elegance. It should be praised by the visitors.

A Woman Washing Clothes was Crushed to Death by a Falling Water Pipe at the Huiquan Bathhouse 179

The Huiquan Bathhouse is located in Chungeng Lane, Shandong Road in this city. At around 7:00 AM yesterday morning, a water pipe from the bathhouse's artesian well water tower, weighing about fifty catties, suddenly fell from a high place. At that time, a twenty-five-year-old Pudong woman, Mrs. Shen Cai, from the Shen Shunchang Ironworks in the lane, was washing clothes next to the water pipe. She was crushed in the head, and blood gushed out instantly. She fell to the ground unconscious. Her son, Shen Erkang, was playing nearby and was also hit in the head. Fortunately, he was spotted by bystanders, who quickly called for an ambulance and sent them to Renji Hospital for treatment. However, Mrs. Shen Cai died at the hospital due to her severe injuries. The matter was immediately reported to the coroner's office for investigation.

Part of the Land Declaration in This City Has Been Completed - Active Land Surveying is Underway 180

Regarding the land declaration, this matter was discussed in detail at the recent financial conference, and an outline has been approved, which will be circulated to all provinces and cities for compliance. However, the land problem in this city is particularly complicated due to the mixture of Chinese and foreigners compared to other places. According to a spokesperson for the Land Bureau of this city, speaking to a reporter from the Central News Agency, part of the land declaration in this city has already been completed due to the collection of temporary land value tax. However, because the Land Law Implementation Regulations have not yet been promulgated, whether the procedures currently performed by the owners should be re-performed in the future depends on whether the method stipulated in the Land Law Implementation Regulations is the same as the existing method. However, according to general practice, land declarations should be held every three years, because land conditions are constantly changing, and the land changes in this city are even more significant than elsewhere. Therefore, if the Land Law Implementation Regulations are promulgated within three years, the land declaration procedures should be re-performed. Currently, this city plans to complete the land survey of the entire city within three years, because handling land declaration matters is closely related to land surveying. Now that the central government is paying special attention to land declaration matters, land surveying in this city will be actively carried out.

German Medical Doctor Huang Cheng Comes to Shanghai - Offering Free Medical Consultations Daily 181

Huang Cheng, a Doctor of Medicine from the University of Berlin in Germany, is erudite and experienced. He studied medicine in Japan for four years and in Germany for twelve years. He holds a highly prestigious national examination diploma from the German medical community. He specializes in rheumatism (diseases such as arthritis) and internal and external departments. He has served as a physician in internal and external (rheumatology) departments at the University Hospital of Berlin and as the director of surgery and venereal diseases at the Furen Hospital in Fuzhou. Later, he went to Germany again to study new treatments in various departments. This spring, he returned to China via Shanghai, bringing newly invented injectable drugs and therapeutic devices. Currently, at the urging and recommendation of prominent Shanghai figures such as Yu Qiaqing, he has established a clinic opposite the General Post Office on Sichuan Road, north of the bridge along the river. The telephone number is 45652. The doctor is known for his compassion and, out of consideration for the poor and sick, offers free medical consultations from 9:00 AM to 10:00 AM every Monday to Friday, waiving the consultation fee. He is truly a blessing to the poor and sick in Shanghai.

Letters 193

To the esteemed Editor:

I am writing to you because I read in your newspaper's local news section yesterday that our station (District 34) was obstructing the New Life Movement and that Yu Zhenhui, a staff member of the Municipal Farmers' Association, was detained by our station and released after the mediation of Pan Mingding, a member of the Municipal Affairs Committee of Gaohang District, and Su Shude, a supervisory committee member of the Fifth District Party Department. This is not in accordance with the facts and concerns the administrative reputation of our station. Therefore, I would like to briefly describe the actual situation on that day. It was found that Yu Zhenhui and others were brought in by Liang Wenlin, the police chief of the downstairs police station, at about 6:00 PM on May 27, who reported that Zhu Hongchang, a member of the Gaohang District Security Corps, and Yu Zhenhui, a staff member of the Municipal Farmers' Association, had a dispute with a local farmer, Sun Fusheng, over a seat while watching a play in Shagang today, and unexpectedly, Yu Zhenhui and others beat the villager Sun Fusheng, causing his head to bleed profusely. He was immediately taken to the rescue team of Qunji Hospital for medication and treatment, and Yu Zhenhui then entered the hospital and beat him again. Fortunately, the director of the hospital dissuaded him, but Yu and others were still angry and wanted to take Sun Fusheng to the Gaohang District Security Corps. Later, Wan Lantian reported the incident, so they were brought to the station together. After investigation, our station learned that Sun Fusheng claimed that he was watching a play in Shagang today, and it was crowded, so he found a high stool. Unexpectedly, Zhu Hongchang, a member of the Gaohang District Security Corps, and Yu Zhenhui, a staff member of the Municipal Farmers' Association, forcibly took the stool. Because he refused to give it up, he was beaten by Yu Zhenhui and others, who falsely accused him of gambling. Yu Zhenhui claimed that he was ordered by the mayor to investigate the New Life Movement in various districts. On the day in question, he was passing through Shagang, Gaoqiao, and saw the villager Sun Fusheng gambling with cigarettes in the theatre so he interferred, leading to the reported contention. But this is a small matter, and he requests forgiveness. (Zhu Hongchang and Yu Zhenhui stated the same.) According to the interrogation, the crime was an injury, and the statements of the plaintiffs and defendants were different, so the case should be resolved by the bureau immediately. However, the head of our station was on official business in Shanghai, so the patrol officer dared not make a decision without authorization. At the same time, Yu Zhenhui and others requested bail, which was immediately granted. The next day, the head of our station returned to the station, and Sun Fusheng came to the station again to ask for justice.

The head of our station immediately ordered the police to summon Yu, but Yu and others hid and did not arrive. This is the actual situation on that day. In addition to reporting the details of the case to the superiors, a corresponding factual letter was sent to your newspaper, hoping that the letter would be published so that the public would be aware of the situation and avoid misunderstandings. Please accept my best wishes for your health. Zhan Chun, the head of the Third District, Dama Police Station, Shanghai Public Security Bureau, respectfully.

Dear Sir,

Yesterday I read in your newspaper that our factory had a fire caused by burning opium paste, but this is not in accordance with the facts. I am writing to you to request a correction in order to maintain our reputation. The actual facts are as follows: Our factory, Wu Hua Chang Machine Factory, has always been located on Haining Road. Because the original building was old, we moved to Shaonian Road last month and have only been there for a month. The wooden house on the cool platform was used to store new and old goods in the machine room. Moreover, the wooden house had only been built for a week, and the carpentry had just been completed, so the appliance had not yet been cleared out. The cause of the fire was probably due to the shop assistants eating and throwing cigarette butts around. The cause of the fire is unknown. The fire occurred at 4:00 AM in the morning, while we were still asleep. We were awakened by the shouts of our neighbors. Your newspaper's report of burning opium paste is shocking. I have never had a smoking habit, so where would the opium paste come from? I believe this is a misrepresentation of the facts. Therefore, I am writing to request a correction. I am deeply grateful. Wu Hua Chang Factory, June 2nd.

Special Article - Refutation of Foreign Misinterpretation of Pilotage Treaty - Declaration of the Preparatory Committee of the Chinese Pilotage Association 194

Since the opening of trade, foreigners have plotted against us. What is obvious on the surface is that they have taken advantage of their power to bully the weak, intimidate with threats, and exploit unequal treaties. But few people know about their many covert tricks and insidious intentions. Their usual methods are nothing more than insinuation and calumny, exploiting the ability to seize by any means. It is found that our country's pilotage sovereignty has not been lost in the treaties in the slightest. The only basis for foreigners to serve as pilots in our country is the Pilotage Regulations approved by the Zongli Yamen by Hart, the Inspector General of Customs, in the seventh year of Tongzhi, which allows both Chinese and foreigners to serve equally. This is an administrative order of the official government and not an international treaty, as everyone knows. However, foreigners intentionally invaded and took an inch further. They colluded with customs commissioners and organized pilotage examination committees in various ports, not allowing Chinese officials to participate, and tried their best to employ foreigners and exclude Chinese people. Not only did the right to examination turn from guest to host, but the more important territorial sovereignty was also invisibly occupied. Obstructed passes and fortresses were freely entered and exited. Military defeats have been suffered in the past, as in the Battle of Mawei in Fujian and Tanggu in Tianjin, where enemy warships were led into the harbor, destroying our navy. More recently, during the January 28th Incident, Japanese warships were led in to fight, inflicting great losses on the 19th Route Army. Afterwards, Philip, the manager of the Shanghai Yangtze Pilotage Association, received the Order of the Rising Sun, as its war honor. The severity of the harm has made people throughout the country grieve with anger. Therefore, there is a consensus that the sovereignty of Chinese pilotage must be recovered as soon as possible in order to eliminate future troubles. On the foreign side, in order to resist, they insinuate that foreigners serving as pilots in our country have a treaty relationship in order to cover up their forcible occupation. This association once published an article in various newspapers on March 17 of this year to make careful corrections. However, the Oriental Affairs Monthly published by foreigners in this port, in its April issue, published an article entitled "Shanghai Pilots," which still forcefully argued and distorted the meaning of the treaty. Therefore, misinterpretations were made to confuse the public and numb people's hearts. This association is afraid that these accumulated errors will become true, so it must be refuted. Therefore, the outline is described, followed by a translation, and then a declaration, so that readers can understand the ins and outs, and distinguish between right and wrong. It is not a concern that the words are too long. Now, let us cite the translation, which says:

The Shanghai Times of March 17 published a message saying that the Shanghai Pilots Association (Chinese) had made a public statement to the effect that the Chinese government had never allowed foreigners to occupy the right to pilot in Chinese territorial waters in any treaty. This declaration was made in response to rumors that the Consular Corps was meeting on the pilotage issue and arguing that the issue should be decided by the countries concerned. The Chinese Pilotage Association further stated that the Chinese government had decided to recover the pilotage rights currently enjoyed by foreigners. (Unfinished)

Readers' Questions and Answers

How to Write a Diary—Answering Mr. Wang Zaifu— 195

Mr. Wang wrote, inquiring about how to write a diary. He said that whenever he tries to write a diary, he always feels that there is nothing to write, and thus doubts the effectiveness of diary writing in self-cultivation. To answer this question, first, we must strengthen Mr. Wang's confidence in writing a diary; second, we must find out the reasons why he encounters difficulties.

Writing a diary plays an extremely important role in the process of studying, which should be acknowledged by anyone with a little experience in studying. On one hand, it can train writing skills; on the other hand, it can gradually expand one's thinking. At the same time, if it is regarded as a record of life, it can encourage oneself and spur oneself to move towards the future one should pursue.

We know that ordinary people cannot freely wield their pens when writing articles. This is not only because of the constraints of the subject matter, but also because the article is written for others to read, and great efforts are often required in phrasing and sentence construction. This leads to the phenomenon that it is not the author who uses the words, but the words that drive the author, creating a clear separation between the words and the content. In reality, words cannot express the meaning, and may even obscure true feelings and thoughts. Therefore, the author cannot but regard writing as a difficult task. So the ancients said, "Articles are inherently heaven-sent," which is partly based on this situation. This makes it very difficult for beginners to improve, whether in terms of writing skills or thinking. However, writing a diary can completely break all of this!

Writing a diary is extremely free, entirely based on the author's free expression. Its content is the content of the author's entire life. It is the most effective way to cultivate the author's ability to unify writing skills within the content. It gives the author the opportunity to practice writing skills for a long time, without subjecting the author to the slightest constraint of words. Of course, our attitude is serious, but we absolutely do not need any concerns or pretenses. Poor writing is not important, and immature thinking is not important either. We are not writing for others to read, but for ourselves to read; to train ourselves, to review ourselves; to organize and refine our daily lives. If we continue in this way, how can our thinking not develop? Only with organized thinking can we have clear and smooth writing. Writing a diary is definitely the best way for beginners to train their minds and writing skills.

However, why does Mr. Wang always feel that there is nothing to write when writing a diary? We believe that the difficulties Mr. Wang encounters are due to the following reasons:

First, he regards diary writing only as a tool for practicing writing skills. He has not broken the concept of viewing writing as a daunting task, so he often struggles to search for words and sentences, while turning a blind eye to daily life, or not daring to bring his own mundane life content to the tip of his pen. These are all mistakes! We absolutely do not believe that a modern person has no life to record. Mr. Wang is a shop apprentice, so the people Mr. Wang comes into contact with are very complex, and the things he experiences will definitely not be simple. Are these not all materials for a diary? Are these materials not enough for Mr. Wang to use? But the reason why Mr. Wang has nothing to write is that as soon as he picks up a pen, he puts all his attention on the use of words, constantly harboring the fear that his words are not enough, so he feels that writing "this" is not good, and writing "that" is not possible, and as a result, many materials slip away from under his pen. Mr. Wang must have read some famous people's diaries, thinking that their diaries are all outstanding works with every word like a pearl. But this is not the case. What they are selling is not goods that have been sealed and untouched, but refurbished counterfeits. "These" are not worth imitating, and should not scare oneself away.

Second, he limits the content of the diary to personal private life. Furthermore, he isolates his private life from society. In this way, the diary becomes nothing more than a personal record of daily life, and when writing, apart from the rigid routines of what time to get up, what time to sleep, how many times to go to the toilet, how many bowls of rice to eat, etc., one will naturally feel that there is nothing to record. Why should we do this? Can't we broaden our horizons? Our lives may be ordinary, with little change, but can't we obtain infinite new materials from what we see and hear every day, and from books, newspapers, and conversations with friends? We can express our own opinions and feelings on even the most trivial issues, regardless of whether our opinions are right or wrong. When you see a policeman beating a rickshaw puller, do you not have any feelings? When you see a beggar asking for money from a store, do you not have any feelings? If so, your diary material is inexhaustible and inexhaustible, so how can you still feel that there is nothing to write?

Finally, he treats diary writing as a rigid task like eating. Of course, writing a diary is most likely to encourage people to reflect on themselves and understand society, because without doing so, there really would be nothing to write, and it would be meaningless. But conversely, we cannot handle it too mechanically, and should give it a lot of freedom. If one day we really have nothing worth writing about—no true feelings of our own, no true opinions of our own—we should simply not write, without having to fabricate anything, without having to write about eating and sleeping to muddle through. This is completely useless. Otherwise, over a longer period of time, you will inevitably feel difficult and bored, and develop a dislike for writing a diary.

Based on the above explanations, we sincerely hope that readers who are just beginning to write a diary, like Mr. Wang, must remember: in terms of technique, you must develop the habit of writing whatever you want to write, and writing long when you have something to say and short when you have nothing to say. You should never be constrained by phrasing and sentence construction, so as not to hinder the development of thought. In terms of content, you should free yourself from personal life, and treat the things around you, and even the entire social life, as diary material. In this way, you will not encounter obstacles in writing, and you will definitely not encounter the difficulty of having nothing to write again. I wonder if Mr. Wang thinks so?

Liu Changchun's Letter to Wang Lan Explains Reasons for Failure 199

He did not practice hard enough in Shanghai, his body became fat, and his weight increased by ten pounds. (Ping News) According to Wang Lan, Liu Changchun's failure made me extremely suspicious, because the results of this competition were not very high. According to Liu Changchun's strength, he certainly had hope of winning a place. But when the news came, it made people feel infinitely disappointed, because I knew that in order to wipe out his shame and hatred, he had worked hard and persevered for years. It is heartbreaking to encounter an unexpected failure. I received two letters from him in the last ten days, one sent before the competition and one sent after the defeat. The letter before the competition was full of descriptions of how he was supported by others and how he felt a great responsibility. This kind of tense situation was also a reason for his failure. The most recent letter arrived in Ping this morning. It is a self-report of his mood after the defeat and the true cause of his failure. Many people who care about Liu Changchun, I will publish it publicly. The following are Liu Changchun's reasons:

Brother Lan,

It's over, I have been eliminated. I am extremely ashamed. My four-year ambition has been reduced to nothing. Now I don't want to think about anything anymore. I'm just waiting for the public to give me a fair scolding.

The weather was cloudy and hot that day, making it difficult for people to breathe. When I went down to the court, I didn't feel very hot, nor was I afraid of the battle, but I couldn't use any strength when I ran. In the 100-meter start, I was beaten by Yoshioka by two meters, and in the end, there was still a difference of two meters. In the 200-meter start, I was second at 100 meters. Everyone thought that my stamina was good, and I would definitely be able to get first place. I thought so too, but when I reached 30 meters from the finish line, I couldn't use any strength in my whole body. In the end, I was overtaken by the second and third place. The 100 meters was the same. However, according to my usual results in these two events, I am very confident in getting second place in the final, but the strength I used on that day felt uneasy and not suitable. After running, I didn't feel very tired, as if there was still strength I hadn't used. After the game, Ma John and I investigated the reason. It was because I didn't always use full strength in practice in Shanghai, because I was afraid of ruining my legs. As a result, I didn't practice hard enough, so my body became fat. Originally, my body weighed 138 pounds, but now it is 148 pounds, plus the hot weather, so I couldn't use my strength. My name will be scolded for thousands of years, and I will have no day to wipe out my shame in this life. Now I don't watch any games anymore, I'm just waiting to be scolded when I return to the country. I wish you well. Your brother Changchun bows his head, May 17th

After Chi Chih (Hold to Purpose) College's Membership Was Revoked From the Joint Sports Meet of Various Independent Colleges 229

Law and Politics and Other Schools Raise Protests

According to a letter from the Law and Politics College volleyball team, Chi Chih College was revoked from membership in the Shanghai Joint Sports Meet of Various Independent Colleges for failing to pay membership fees. The number of participating schools has suddenly decreased, which is obviously inconsistent with the original resolution. Currently, Law and Politics and other schools have jointly sent a letter to the Organizing Committee requesting a re-drawing of lots for the competition. The reason stated is that Chi Chih also attended the second meeting of representatives of various schools for ball games at the Zhengfeng Literature College. At that time, including Chi Chih, a total of seven schools participated in the volleyball competition. After mutual consultation among the school representatives, it was decided to determine the competition schedule by drawing lots. Now that Chi Chih has failed to pay membership fees and its membership has been revoked, the previous resolution has therefore changed. If the old plan is implemented again, it would be obviously illegal. It is hoped that your committee will immediately convene a general meeting of representatives from various schools to discuss again. It is reported that the letter has now been submitted to the Organizing Committee, and various schools believe that its reasons are justified and have expressed their support.

Education News

Detailed Record of the Jiangsu Provincial Middle School Education Conference 240

(Zhenjiang Correspondent) The Jiangsu Provincial Federation of Secondary School Teachers and Staff held an education conference at Zhenjiang Normal School yesterday (the 1st) morning at 9:00 AM. More than 20 representatives from various schools, including Xia Peibai, Liu Mengjin, and Wu Zier, attended. More than 30 important cases were resolved, and the meeting adjourned late at night. The important cases are selected and listed as follows:

(1) How should students in senior and junior high schools and various vocational schools who wish to pursue further education or service due to changes in environment or interests be remedied? (Resolution 1: For the current first-year students in junior high school, elective courses in vocational fields should be set up to facilitate students' education. 2: For the current first and second-year students in senior high school and vocational schools, elective courses should be set up to meet the needs. 3: Please ask teachers to set up supplementary schools to provide remedies. (2) The children's army training in rural normal schools should be abolished, and all the time should be changed to military training to save the country from peril. (Resolution) Passed and submitted to the Education Department. (3) Please request the Education Department to devise ways to compile and improve textbooks for each subject that conform to the progress table for application in the 23rd year. (Resolution) Passed. (4) How should the difficulties in implementing the progress table for each subject be remedied? (Resolution) Handled in conjunction with the third case. (5) The use of original textbooks for physics and chemistry makes it difficult for students to learn and reduces educational efficiency. How should this be remedied? (Resolution) In addition to referring to the resolutions of previous science conferences, the Education Department is requested to compile textbooks on mathematics, physics, and chemistry as soon as possible. After the publication of these textbooks, the Education Department is urged to strictly prohibit the use of English textbooks in all schools. (6) The teaching time for history in the senior high school normal department seems insufficient in terms of curriculum. The original standard should be changed and slightly increased. (Resolution) Submit to the Ministry of Education to change the history teaching time of normal schools to a 4-1 system to facilitate teaching. (7) The methods for awarding scholarships to poor students should be promulgated and revised and interpreted. (Resolution) Request the Education Department to interpret and promote the minimum standards for excellent and physically fit students and add "those with an average grade of 60 points and no failing grades." (8) The middle school entrance examination set by the Education Department should be revised. (Resolution) If the Education Department uses a unified method for the enrollment of various schools, the Association does not express any opinion. If the entrance examination is still held separately by each school, the usual practice will be followed, with special emphasis on the four subjects stipulated by the Education Department. As for the Education Department's method of allocating the number of students admitted to normal schools by region, it can only be used as a reference. (9) Review the regulations on student promotion and retention, supplementary examinations, and academic performance assessment promulgated by the Ministry and submit them to the Education Department. (Resolution) Recommend the Suzhou Middle School, Suzhou Women's Normal School, and Suzhou Agricultural School to review and submit them to the Executive Committee of the Education Association within one week. (10) In the 13th year, schools at all levels in the province are promoting production education and reducing the number of ordinary middle school and normal department classes. However, vocational schools do not enroll students, but the number of junior high school graduates is increasing day by day, making it difficult to enter schools. Can the Association request the Education Department to designate existing schools to add vocational training classes or allow various career schools to enroll both male and female students to avoid students missing out? (Resolution) Passed. (11) How should ability grouping be implemented to achieve practical teaching? (Resolution) In groups with lower levels, additional class time should be added to equalize the levels. (12) Junior high schools should implement military formation, and senior high schools should implement military training formation to cultivate a disciplined life and conform to the spirit of combining education and training. (Resolution) Passed. (13) How should ideological guidance for senior high school students be implemented? (Resolution) A. Ideological tests and surveys. B. Individual guidance and talks. C. Actively guiding reading materials and assignments. D. Holding systematic civic lectures. (14) The report form on academic and conduct status is not practical. Should the Education Department be requested to abolish its use? (Resolution) Recommend the Suzhou Middle School and Suzhou Women's Normal School to revise it and submit it to the Education Association for adoption.

Joint Announcement by the Education and Industry Departments - Labor Education Incentive Rules 241

The Education and Industry Departments jointly announced five articles of the Labor Education Incentive Rules yesterday. The articles are as follows: (Article 1) These rules are formulated in accordance with the provisions of Article 20 of the Outline of Implementation Measures for Labor Education. (Article 2) All labor education conducted by factories, companies, stores, public and private organizations shall be awarded incentives in accordance with the following regulations: (1) Those who train more than 200 workers annually, with expenses exceeding 1,000 yuan, and achieve remarkable results shall be awarded a fifth-class certificate of merit. (2) Those who train more than 300 workers annually, with expenses exceeding 1,500 yuan, and achieve good results shall be awarded a fourth-class certificate of merit. (3) Those who train more than 400 workers annually, with expenses exceeding 2,000 yuan, and achieve remarkable results shall be awarded a third-class certificate of merit. (4) Those who train more than 500 workers annually, with expenses exceeding 2,500 yuan, and achieve outstanding results shall be awarded a second-class certificate of merit. (5) Those who train more than 600 workers annually, with expenses exceeding 3,000 yuan, and achieve remarkable results shall be awarded a first-class certificate of merit. (6) Those who train more than 1,000 workers annually, with expenses exceeding 5,000 yuan, and achieve remarkable results shall be awarded a first-class certificate of merit and a plaque. (Article 3) Certificates of merit and plaques shall be issued jointly by the Industry and Education Departments. (Article 4) Those who have been awarded prizes in accordance with these rules shall not apply for prizes separately in accordance with the Regulations on Donations to Schools by the National Government. (Article 5) These rules shall be jointly promulgated by the Industry and Education Departments.

The Public Works Department Discusses School Subsidy Issues 244

The subsidy of the Public Works Department to private Chinese schools within the concession, except for two schools, has been decided to be distributed immediately for the first quarter of this year. The Education Committee also decided that, starting in 1935, foreign schools applying for subsidies should first investigate their needs, then submit them to the sub-committee for review, and also have the Hygiene and Public Works Departments add their comments, and then allocate the funds proportionally. As for schools that have already received subsidies, they should be asked to report clearly whether they have been spent for the designated purpose and submit receipts to verify the facts.

The Sanitation Department believes that the sanitation equipment improvement fees given to some schools far exceed their needs. Although the funds they received were all used to improve cleanliness, they exceeded the work specified by the Sanitation Department. Therefore, schools should be asked to report this matter in detail. The Director of Education then suggested that schools requesting subsidies in the future should first be investigated by the Director of Chinese Education to clarify their needs and notify the sub-committee, and then the relevant administrative departments should add their opinions before allocating the subsidies. The committee members agreed with this proposal and decided to do the same for foreign schools.

Regarding those who rent houses to set up schools, the Sanitation Department has conducted investigations into the existence and duration of leases, and will then make suggestions on whether or not to grant sanitation improvement fees and the amount.

Regarding the use of subsidies for school libraries, the sub-committee has given it careful consideration. In general, the granting of funds is not taken as a precedent for the following year. Also, the use of subsidies to purchase experimental equipment is considered appropriate because natural science is part of the middle and primary school curriculum.
