Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly

How to Read Books? 246

According to my investigation, children under the age of eight do not understand how to protect books. Children around the age of eight cherish their books very much. When they buy a new book, they carefully wrap the cover with paper and are careful not to damage or stain it. They are also very careful when reading it. This attitude of cherishing books is undoubtedly commendable and should be promoted.

However, children should understand that cherishing books is one thing, and reading books is another. Do not let cherishing books hinder reading. What does this mean? For example, when reading an unfamiliar word, feel free to underline it. Do not refrain from underlining it because you are afraid of staining the book. You should know that underlining provides some help in terms of reading methods. Books are ultimately for people to read, not for decoration. Cherishing is ultimately a minor matter. Therefore, I advise children to do three things when reading: First, underline unfamiliar words to calculate how many unfamiliar words you recognize each day and to know the ratio of reading to recognizing unfamiliar words. Second, circle or dot your favorite sentences or sentences with important meaning. This shows that you have already read this article and makes it easier to understand at a glance. Third, this requires older children who read a lot to be able to do. If you have some opinions when reading something, feel free to add marginal notes at the top of the book. As for whether the opinions are correct or not, you do not have to worry about it, because the teacher will correct any errors in thinking.

Finally, I will reiterate: Do not let cherishing books hinder reading.

Model Children of the New Life Movement 247

— Da Zhai

Propriety Confucius played as a child, arranging sacrificial vessels (i.e., ritual utensils) and practicing rituals. Later, Confucius taught his son Boyu to learn propriety, saying, "If you do not learn propriety, you will have nothing to stand on." Therefore, Boyu also learned propriety.

Righteousness When Washington was eighteen, he was doing surveying work by the Potomac River. A four-year-old child nearby fell into the water. Everyone was afraid to rescue him because the current was too strong. Washington bravely jumped into the river. Despite the danger, he was rescued. He had such a spirit of public service since childhood, so only Washington could be competent as the President of the American Revolutionary War.

Integrity Lincoln was an extremely poor child in his youth. Someone recommended him to be a manager of a cargo store. Once, he miscalculated a woman by four cents. After the market closed in the evening, he walked two or three miles to return it. Another time, he gave someone half a pound of tea less. That night, there was a great storm with thunder. No one was walking on the road. He carried half a pound of tea and walked a long way to return it to the person. People only know him as the savior who liberated black slaves. It turns out that although his childhood environment was poor, his behavior was very honest.

Shame The Germans once succumbed to the iron hooves of Napoleon. After the Franco-Prussian War, the German army triumphed. Bismarck said: "Our success today is all due to the hard work of elementary school teachers who have cultivated many good children over the years. That's why we have these loyal and brave soldiers." It can be seen that to save the country from difficulties, all children in the country must not forget the national humiliation.

Little Laborers 248

— Shi Yusheng

Dark red, light red, yellow, white, clusters and clumps, are displayed in the garden, are peaches, apricots, crabapples, roses... there are also some unknown flowers. Draped in the light yarn of the morning sun, they are even more charming and beautiful. Waves of fragrance are sprayed out, rippling in the silent air.

Buzz, buzz, buzz, branches and flowers, entangled with many small things. They busily burrow into the flowers, spreading their wings, extending their beaks, trying to suck something. Suddenly, with a "whoosh" sound, they flew back to their nests, singing triumphant mountain songs.

Children, what are these little things, and what are they busy with?

吧！

High! High! High! Flying High! — The New Air Route — 249

— Eagle

Airplanes! Are what children love to look up at the most. Flying! Is what the new youth of the twentieth century are most proud of. But pilots in the sky often encounter clouds and fog covering the sky and the earth, losing their sense of direction and unable to see the route, which is very dangerous. Sometimes encountering strong winds and heavy rain in the air is like a lonely boat trapped in the waves of the sea, making it impossible to steer, which is also extremely dangerous.

Scientists, in order to reduce the dangers of aviation and find a safe route for pilots, are now about to succeed in their experiment!

Where is this new air route?

It turns out that the upper layer of the atmosphere, about eleven kilometers above the ground, is called the "stratosphere." There, there are no clouds or fog (because it is above the clouds and fog), no lightning or thunderstorms, and no changes in cold or heat (the temperature is always stable, so it is called the stratosphere). Airplanes flying in this high atmospheric layer will travel several times faster than ordinary flights.

Therefore, future aviation will not only be very safe but also very fast. According to the latest record set by French pilot Der Motte, the average speed is 431 kilometers per hour. It is predicted that in the future, it will be possible to fly 1,000 kilometers per hour in the stratosphere!

Ambitious children! Our thoughts should turn to the sky!

Silkworm, Shanghai Weida Primary School Student 250

— Yang Jiaying

Little silkworms are called treasures, they only eat mulberry leaves and not rice.

The weather is good in spring, and the treasures develop early.

The silkworm girls in the east village are busy, the farmers' wives in the west village are busy, picking mulberry leaves to fill the baskets, filling the baskets with mulberry leaves to feed the silkworms, and the silkworms' bodies are strong.

Spinning silk and making cocoons is a good job, making the farmers laugh heartily.

Once the farming is busy, the silkworm business is over, carrying the cocoons to the neighborhood, exchanging them for gold and silver, buying fish, buying meat, and buying grain, all saying that the silkworms are good.

Human Weapons 251

— Ban Wen

I once wrote an article in this publication about the weapons of fish, describing how fish rely on their unique weapons to defend themselves against other creatures that threaten their lives. At the end, I also asked the children: "What are your weapons?"

Now I tell you: your weapon is "knowledge." At your age, you are all starting to acquire simple "knowledge," because humans need "knowledge" to survive.

The great American philosopher John Dewey once said: "Knowledge is authority," which means that humans have "knowledge" and therefore have the authority to survive. Fish are lower-level creatures, and their weapons rely solely on sharp teeth, spines, tails, etc., which is because they lack "knowledge." Since we humans are higher-level creatures, our weapons should be more civilized and also the most effective.

Dear children, quickly cultivate the seeds of "knowledge," they will sprout and eventually bear fruit. Do not be lazy for a moment and fail to taste the sweetness of the fruit!

Your weapon is "knowledge"!

Children, please remember this sentence I say today.

The World in a Box 252

— Yu Bailu

If you are willing to do as I say, then the box you make will definitely contain the world. The method is as simple as described below.

Tools and Materials: One cigarette box that holds 225 cigarettes, one sheet of white paper, plus a pen and ink.

Instructions: Use the pen to paint the inside of the entire box black with ink. After it dries, paste the white paper in the middle of the box, dividing it into two pairs of rectangles of equal size. Then, use a needle to prick a tiny hole in one end of the box, and use scissors to cut a hole the size of two hairmark in the other end. Then, close the lid (the inside of the lid must also be painted with ink). This box is now complete.

How to Play: Hold the box in your hand, close one eye, and keep the other eye open (if you cannot do this, or if doing this makes your eyes feel very uncomfortable, then you can hold the box with one hand and cover your eye with the other hand). Look through the hole made by the scissors, and the outside world will be reflected on the white paper in your box. People and cars will move, but they will be upside down.

What is the reason for this? Children may want to ask me, but here, because of your knowledge and the length of the newspaper, I cannot tell you anything for the time being. Telling you will only confuse you. Fortunately, in the near future, physics will tell you thoroughly and clearly. Regarding this point, I only hope that all the children will study hard.

The Pile of Stones in Our Schoolyard 253

— Chu Jianping

The pile of stones in our schoolyard has been there for three years now. Now I will write down its origin, please all the children read it quietly.

One day, a third-grade student in Group B in our school was holding a rubber cat in his hand, squeezing it and playing with it, looking very proud.

"This is a foreign product! How can you be so unpatriotic?" As soon as I saw it, I rebuked him like this.

"What does it matter? It's only two cents in total. Even if they take it, they won't get rich, and we won't become poor!" He argued with me very reasonably. I knew from his tone that without factual evidence, I couldn't reason with him. So, I immediately informed all the students that from the next day onwards, when coming to school, each person must pick up a stone on the road and throw it in the designated place in the schoolyard, without forgetting or interrupting. Although they all felt confused, they had to do as instructed.

After a week, the pile of stones was more than three feet high. I pointed to the pile of stones and asked the student who had been playing with the little cat, "Can you still say that two cents doesn't matter now? Look! There are only a little over a hundred people in our school, and the small stones accumulated in a week are already so high. If 400 million Chinese people all give two cents to the Japanese, how much do you think that total would be?" In this way, all the students in the school understood.

Swatting Flies 257

— Wang Shouqiu

The weather is gradually getting warmer, and the flies that people hate the most are gradually appearing. Although flies are very small things, they can transmit epidemics, and countless people lose their lives because of them every year. Therefore, flies are our enemies, and we should exterminate them. The reproduction of flies is extremely fast. Roughly speaking, one fly now will become hundreds of thousands, or even millions, of flies in the future. If we kill one fly now, it is like killing hundreds of thousands, or millions, of flies in the future. Therefore, now is the time for us to swat flies. I hope that after class, children will engage in fly-swatting work, which is very important for hygiene and cleanliness. However, flies cannot be swatted with objects but must be swatted with fly swatters made of green gauze. Furthermore, the dead flies must be burned in the fire, and after swatting, the fly swatter must be hidden well, and you must never touch it with your hands, because fly swatters are very dirty. Children should pay special attention to this point. Also, after swatting flies, you should wash your hands clean before eating anything. Children! Let's all engage in fly-swatting work!

Why Do Insects Molt? 258

— Xu Chajie

Insects, snakes, crabs...and many other insects, they must molt once every time they grow. When molting, the old epidermis is removed from the root, and a new epidermis is regenerated. When you children see it, you must feel why they are not afraid of pain, and are not afraid of trouble, and must do this. In fact, they have no choice!

The epidermis of insects and snakes contains lime and will only harden, not expand. The inside of the insect's body grows day by day, and the epidermis binds it, making it really uncomfortable, so it sheds the old epidermis and produces another layer of wide epidermis. The molting of insects is really a physiological relationship for them!

Commercial News

Yarn and Cotton Prices Surge, with High-Grade Yarn at 188.4 and Cotton at 47.20; Trading Volume Reaches 133,200 Bales of Yarn and 273,700 Loads of Cotton 260

The yarn market continues its bullish run, with prices surging dramatically. This is largely due to pent-up demand being unleashed after a long period of stagnation. News of a severe drought in the United States has pushed up U.S. cotton prices, forcing short sellers to cover their positions at a loss. Market sentiment is extremely volatile. However, yarn sales have slowed down somewhat due to the high prices. Nevertheless, rising cotton prices are fueling the surge in yarn prices.

In pre-market trading, speculative yarn prices rose in response to higher prices for imported cotton. Buying activity was intense, with prices for all months rising by 1.2, 3, or 4 yuan. The afternoon session opened flat, but prices suddenly surged in the second and third rounds of trading, with prices for all months rising by 1.7, 9 jiao, or 2 to 2.3 or 4 yuan. The sentiment among both bulls and bears in the market was uncertain, leading to a significant increase in trading volume. Total trading volume for the day reached 133,200 bales, with sales from Da Ji (1,900 bales), Da Feng (3,500 bales), Zhen Da (1,450 bales), Hui Kang (1,800 bales), Rui Da (2,400 bales), Jun Chang (1,650 bales), Yuan Feng (1,450 bales), Ren Feng (2,300 bales), Da Yi (1,200 bales), Tai Chang (1,300 bales), Chang Feng (4,650 bales), Xie Sheng (2,300 bales), Xin Cheng (1,850 bales), Chang Yu (1,350 bales), Yuan Tai (1,100 bales), and Da Chang (1,450 bales). U.S. Cotton Awaits Developments in Washington 264

A telegram from New York on June 1st reported on the cotton market for the week, stating that the cotton market was very quiet last week, with prices fluctuating. Industry peers are awaiting developments in Washington. At the same time, there is a conflicting sentiment, because on the one hand, the new cotton is good and the demand for cotton is not good, but on the other hand, the supply in the South is small and there are often changes in the new cotton during the summer. Trading volume is extremely thin, with few bulls closing positions and few speculative sales. The threat of boll weevils is indeed developing in the southwestern cotton region, but there have been no reports in the eastern region. However, the extent of the damage is not yet significant. Planting is 95% complete, and 85% of the crop is developing well. Agricultural authorities announced that the tax under the Peng Hai-min proposal will be based on a price of 1 jiao, 1 fen, and 3 li and 4 hao, which means that excess production will be taxed 5 fen, 6 li, and 7 hao per pound.

Financial Silver Party Plots to Abolish Silver Tax, Spot Gold Falls Slightly by 2.40 Yuan – Market Situation Stable then Weak in the Morning Session – 265

Yesterday, the gold market was slightly volatile due to rumors that the pro-silver faction in the U.S. Senate was moving to abolish the 50% tax on silver transaction profits proposed by the President. However, this did not have a significant impact. Although prices fell, the market situation remained stable in the morning session. At the beginning of the day, overseas silver markets in both the UK and the U.S. declined, with forward silver prices on the Gold Exchange falling by 1 to 2 li. Exchange rates did not fluctuate much. London spot gold rose by 2 pence, U.S. cotton rose by 27 points, and U.S. wheat declined slightly. An Associated Press dispatch stated that pro-silver senators Thomas, Wheeler, and Borah were planning a meeting to discuss abolishing the 50% tax on silver profits. Initial off-market trading showed a slight decline, which then stabilized. After the market opened, prices trended downward. HSBC's listed prices for both UK and U.S. currency were flat and then declined further, but market sentiment remained relatively stable with much fluctuation. A Reuters dispatch stated that the U.S. would announce the issuance of new bonds worth $1,000,000,000 next Monday. The overall trend remained low. After entering the market, domestic prices stabilized, but trading was light, causing the market to fluctuate without much change. Near noon, major players showed strong buying interest, with demand exceeding supply, leading to repeated rebounds. However, many were willing to sell at higher prices. The market closed lower. There were rumors in the market that silver prices would rise in the night session, primarily due to profit-taking on the eve of Sunday. Overall, the fluctuations were narrow, and trading was quite ordinary. The price of pure gold was 1039.3 yuan. The market situation for the morning session is recorded below:

The morning opening price was 1029.3 yuan, a slight increase of 1 jiao compared to the previous closing price. Goods opened at the same price. For a long time after that, prices fluctuated around 7 yuan. Zhengjin took delivery of September U.S. dollars at 9375 and then rose to 7.3 yuan. Dadecheng, Yuqingyong, Fuxingyong, and Gong Tiao fell again to 6.4 yuan. Hengyu, Yifengyong, and Tongchun accepted Tiao and rebounded. Yukang bought aggressively, rising again to 7.9 yuan. New York Stock Prices Fall 270

Xinfeng Foreign Firm reports that yesterday (the 1st) the New York Stock Exchange market was almost stagnant all day due to a lack of stimulating news. In the end, many wheat bulls rushed to liquidate their profits, creating a surge in selling, and wheat prices fell sharply. Stock prices were also active, falling drastically by more than 3 yuan. However, the wheat-growing regions remain dry. The minor exchange saw mixed results with a slight decrease. Bonds were also weak, but Argentine public bonds rose again. Cotton rose by more than 1.5 yuan, as news indicated that Congress was likely to pass the Smith Act, authorizing the government to purchase 150 million yuan worth of cotton for relief. If so, then each yarn factory will be busy with work in the summer, and labor unrest may be eliminated. The (securities) market remains stagnant, continuing to trend downward. (Wheat) The public continues to enter, and bulls are liquidating their profits. The public will re-enter when prices fall. The drought has not decreased, and market declines will elicit support from all sides. The weather in the wheat-growing regions has not changed, remaining hot and dry. The market situation may experience a reaction due to rain and excessive buying. However, according to many opinions, the ultimate price level will be high. (Cotton) Prices rose due to extreme heat in several western areas, the possibility of the drought spreading, and poor harvests in Soviet Russia. The above all indicate the market's reactive trends rather than significant developments. Field crops are progressing smoothly, and no rain in June will benefit most cotton crops. Factory purchases totaled 195,000 bales this week. The spot market is stagnant, and cloth is quiet. (Rubber) Prices rose due to firmness in major markets, buying by industry peers, and news of restrictions on the number of exports from Batavia. (Silver) The market remains dull.

Grain Flour Prices Rise Sharply - Forward Prices Up 3 to 4 Points 272

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, prices in each month showed a trend of first falling and then rising. The reported prices for foreign wheat in Chicago and Canada had fallen back by 0.2 to 0.3 yuan. Therefore, market sentiment inside and outside the industry was initially weak when prices opened, falling by 0.05 to 0.1 yuan compared to the previous day. Subsequently, the market rebounded as major outside speculators continued to aggressively buy. This surge by the bulls was entirely due to the poor wheat conditions in the United States and the drought, which simultaneously affected international sentiment. Although the domestic new wheat harvest was abundant and there was selling by actual sales brokers, this could not contain the frenzied price increases. At the afternoon opening, near and forward month trading remained unusually active. It was rumored that Tianjin and small factories were selling, while the Yingkou gang and major local speculators were aggressively buying at each price increase. As most businesses were concentrated in the forward months, the price increases were also bold. The total volume of transactions in the morning and afternoon reached 1.2 to 1.3 million bags, the highest this year. The frenzy of market sentiment was unprecedented since the price declines. As a result, the price in the current month increased by 0.175 yuan, July by 0.15 yuan, August by 0.225 yuan, September by 0.3 yuan, October by 0.475 yuan, and November by 0.35 yuan.

Fluctuations in Forward Wheat Prices 273

Yesterday, the forward wheat market was generally calm after the opening in the morning. Foreign wheat prices in Chicago and Canada fell back slightly by 0.2 to 0.3 yuan. Therefore, market sentiment was mostly cautious, with limited buying and selling. Industry observers had conflicting views, and the wheat harvest was imminent, so the situation was not entirely the same as in the flour market. By the afternoon opening, market sentiment had become frenzied. The morning flour market had been exceptionally good, and prices continued to rise in the afternoon. As a result, prices opened 0.3 to 0.6 yuan higher than the morning. Subsequently, prices fell back as long-term bulls sold and inland brokers dumped their holdings. Industry observers believed that a week from now all new wheat would be on the market, and if sales did not pick up, the future would not be good. As a result, the price in July rose by 0.1 yuan, August and September by 0.2 yuan, and October by 0.3 yuan. Due to inactivity from factories, spot wheat had no market, and old goods were unsalable.

Weak Sales of Ke Xian Rice Stabilize 274

The Ke Xian rice market saw continued arrivals of goods that had been previously shipped from other locations. However, the quantity had decreased, and sellers were less anxious to sell. Some customers saw increased activity in another province and were unwilling to lower prices. However, the other merchants were still loading their previous orders, and no shipping space was available for new orders, so sales actually decreased. Other merchants were waiting and watching, and trading suddenly became quiet. A total of 843 bags of processed and unmilled rice were traded by Fujian merchants, with varying prices, mostly similar to the previous market. However, because the street committee had recommended a rice merchant as the leader of the industry, the rice market in Hexia had been closed for one day. As a result, nearly 1,000 bags of processed and yuan rice were purchased from this street, and the market began to stabilize.

New Jiujiang Rapeseed Opens at 3.8 Yuan 275

Yesterday, the only new goods arriving were a batch of 99 bags of new Jiujiang rapeseed. The quality was medium, with excessive amounts of mud and fine ash, rated between 87 and 80. The price opened at 3.8 yuan. Over 400 bags of Wenzhou goods arrived but were not traded. New broad beans have been harvested in various locations. If the weather remains clear, they will be shipped here next week in succession. Yesterday, merchants purchased 13,800 bags of various soybeans, and telegrams reported rising prices, so sentiment was tight. However, there was little change in prices. The entire market traded one truckload of Zhengyangguan beans and two truckloads of Feihe beans, which were purchased by merchants. Two truckloads of Yingzhou beans were opened, and the factory purchased them.

Silk and Tea Russian Firms Start Trading in Qi Ning Black Tea 276

Yesterday, in the foreign tea market of this port, Russian firms and the Cooperation Association Foreign Firm have begun trading in black tea from Qimen and Ningzhou. British firms such as Jardine Matheson, Cooper, and Tianyu have also taken the opportunity to replenish their stocks. As a result, the price of black tea, which had been declining, has stabilized. According to tea merchants, the sales of Russian black tea seem to be as large as in previous years. The reason is that the prices of Indian and Ceylonese tea are high, Russian goods imported to China have increased sharply, and there have been financial and credit issues. Since the violent price drop the day before yesterday, the green tea market has also seen quite active trading.

New Silkworm Cocoon Prices in Jiangsu and Zhejiang Difficult to Increase 277

Farmers in Pingyao Suffer Losses Farmers in the Pingyao area suffered damage from the weather to their early native silkworms and are now raising improved late silkworms. Hatching is delayed, and the silkworms eat more leaves. Although the late silkworm harvest is more abundant, the cocoons are also superior to the early native silkworm cocoons, but the cocoon costs are not low. The cocoon markets have been open for many days, but cocoon prices have been restricted by public discussion and cannot be freely traded. Improved silkworm cocoons are only 25 to 26 yuan, and native silkworm cocoons are 15 to 16 yuan. Prices on the Sima scale are only 31 to 32 yuan and 18 to 19 yuan, respectively. Farmers are suffering heavy losses.

Many Silk Reels in Xiashi Xiashi has always been a famous silk-producing area. This year, farmers have raised a strong number of silkworms and have had good harvests. However, there are too many silkworms and too few leaves, and leaf prices have been very high, reaching 2.5 to 2.6 yuan. Farmers' silkworm costs have been over 40 yuan. The cocoon markets are opening and offering only 30 yuan for superior improved silkworm cocoons and 20 yuan for native silkworm cocoons. Each load of fresh cocoons must be sold at a loss of over 10 yuan, so they are all reeling their own silk.

Haiyan New Cocoon Prices Opening Kanghai peasants of the four villages raised sericulture this spring, lost considerable native species in transit, and improved breeds performed quite well. New cocoons have come onto the market, and are about 80% full. Few cocoon markets have opened, and cocoon prices are low. Improved cocoon market price is only 25 to 26 yuan city scale, land species is 14 or 15 yuan. Farmers are difficult to earn a profit, and even leaf costs are not covered.

Henglin Cocoon Market Opening Soon The Donghenglin improved silkworm area of this state is where farmers are largely raising improved species this year, where guidance has been effective, and achievements have been excellent. Early silk worms may soon be down from the raised platforms, and a bountiful harvest is to be expected. Gonghe Yong, and other cocoon operations are expected to start their openings gradually as of tomorrow, prices for cocoons will be publicly negotiated, improved cocoons will be at a maximum of 25 or 26 yuan, native varieties will be at 15 yuan, by city scale.

Shuang Gong Silk India Demand Not Weak The India need for Shuang Gong silk is still abundant, Fulan Heng Shuang Gong silk factory is actively processing to reel old cocoons with newly arriving domestic cocoons. Shuang Gong silk is therefore more easily exported, and over the latter half of the month, 158 bales shipped to England, transferred onward to India.

Tin Spot Price Loitering Without Improving 278

Spot Tin is unmoving because the avenue for sales is dead, there's little activity in the market, and prices aren't high. Malaysian grades open at 191 or 192 yuan, Dutch grades at 215 or 216 yuan, and Thai grades at 200 yuan. Transactions are occasional, with few purchases. Exports and large volume business face a situation of loitering and not improving.

Women's Realm

Advocating for Pregnant Working Women 279

— Bi Yao

Forcing pregnant women who are seven or eight months along to continue laborious work as usual is something that should not happen in a civilized, organized human society. However, like other forms of encroachment, exploitation, and oppression – various things that should not exist – this still persists in current society.

If a married woman abandons her family responsibilities and the nurturing of her children to seek meager income in various institutions and factories, then there is undoubtedly a ravenous wolf of survival chasing her. This forces her to risk suffering and danger for a monthly wage of three, five, or a little over ten yuan. Even when her belly is large, she must still stagger into and out of the work gates. It is not because she is inherently greedy, but because that ravenous wolf will not ease up on her even as she nears delivery.

Although precise statistics are currently unavailable, the number of miscarriages, difficult births, or deaths caused by excessive work among pregnant working women is undoubtedly shockingly large. Where does one even begin to address this?

Some more enlightened institutions give female teachers and female staff of higher professional status one month of pre- and postnatal leave with regular pay. However, female factory workers and domestic servants of lower status not only do not receive such preferential treatment, but they also worry about losing their jobs to others during the few days of unpaid rest after giving birth.

The work of domestic servants is sometimes light and sometimes heavy, with varying degrees of intermittency. The most unbearable is the work of female factory workers, who are not allowed a single second of rest within fixed working hours. A pregnant woman in this situation is in a worse position than in hell. What have they done to wrong the factory owners on a daily basis? Among female workers in mechanized industries, the work rate of female workers is not weaker than that of male workers, yet the difference in wages often reaches a factor of one. Most female factory workers are currently unmarried. How many women in a factory become pregnant each year? Using the profits from their usual wages to subsidize a few pregnant women so that they can rest before and after childbirth is only natural.

People in our country are always talking about propriety, justice, and the ethical order. In fact, those who adhere to ritual teachings are the least moral. Customarily, there are the so-called four taboos: first, moving west of a dwelling is taboo; second, it's taboo to see a woman breastfeeding; fourth, it’s taboo to hold a child born in the first or fifth lunar month. Even in today’s feudal society, scholars still do not step into the bedroom of a woman in childbirth, even when his own wife is on the verge of death. Women giving birth to children is inherently sacred work beneficial to humanity, yet scholars and officials regard it as ominous and taboo it. How much they despise women's flesh and blood! How much they belittle their own origins!

Due to the traditional contempt for women's childbirth, coupled with cruel exploitation, the issue of pregnant women still working desperately as usual when nearing delivery has become a non-issue.

Turning all problematic things into non-issues is inherently easy; all one needs to do is close one's eyes and one will not see black and white. However, if this happens, everyone will become blind. This is not only the misfortune of pregnant working women; what about the culture of the Chinese nation? What about the survival of the Chinese nation?

The issue of paid rest for pregnant working women before and after childbirth is a small piece of many issues, and it does not affect major events in all aspects. As long as everyone does not completely ignore it, as long as at least some humanitarianism exists in people's hearts, it is hoped that society can enthusiastically promote and agitate for it so that it can be implemented universally as soon as possible!

Examining with Mr. Chen Da the Urgent Need for Birth Control in China 280

— Zi Jiu

The May 4th issue of the Ta Kung Pao published an article by Professor Chen Da of Tsinghua University, titled "The Need for Birth Control in China," which he delivered as a speech at the Rotary Club in Beiping. Because of Mr. Chen's reputation and the startling nature of the topic, it drew my special attention. However, after reading the speech, I felt compelled to speak out. Everyone knows that the entire China has fallen into the tragic state of poverty, ignorance, disease, and death, under the combined attack of natural disasters and human calamities. However, the reason for this is not overpopulation, but poor governance and a deteriorating environment. Mr. Chen does not grasp the core of the problem, abandoning the fundamental to pursue the superficial, saying: "To prevent disasters before they happen, there is an urgent need to control births, thereby reducing suffering and improving the nation." Mr. Chen made this grand pronouncement because he was shocked by the report of the relief association, which stated that "there are 60 million disaster victims in fourteen provinces of China." Here, based on the records of the Ta Kung Pao, I will discuss and examine Mr. Chen's points as follows:

Reducing Mortality

We believe that what is causing the current terrible mortality rate in China is not overpopulation or excessive births. However, Mr. Chen says: "If we can reach the level of the Irish birth rate, then the number of births each year can be reduced to seven million, and the number of deaths each year can be reduced from twelve million to five million." Even if we disregard whether the health administration and public intelligence of Ireland are compatible with China, the fact is that before domestic and foreign troubles are eliminated, natural disasters will not be reduced by human effort, and the deaths of the people will only increase, not decrease. If most people listen to Mr. Chen's theory, on the one hand, the birth rate will be greatly reduced, and on the other hand, the population will still be rapidly dying. Will the Chinese nation not be completely eliminated? Since ancient times, there have only been countries that perished due to population decline, and there has never been an example of a country perishing due to population increase.

Children's Education

Mr. Chen said: "In 1925, the percentage of children enrolled in school in England was about 93% of the school-age children, while in China, according to the Ministry of Education's report, the proportion was only 9%. If we want to improve the quality of the population, we naturally need to reduce births." Can reducing births really improve the quality of the population? We know that the development of education is the responsibility of the government. The government collects large amounts of educational taxes from the people every year to establish schools. In this reality of widespread illiteracy, we can only passively urge the government to quickly improve the current education system to seek opportunities for everyone to receive education. Mr. Chen's intention seems to be to forcefully cut the number of existing and future children to 9%, allowing this small number of people to enjoy educational opportunities. Isn't this "cutting the feet to fit the shoes"? Look at India and Annam, where the population is decreasing day by day, but their culture is not increasing with each passing day. I do not want to use a subjugated nation as a metaphor, but I use this to prove that education relies entirely on political power to promote it.

Raising Living Standards

Mr. Chen's main idea is that "Chinese workers have too little income and cannot afford the cost of children's education. Reducing births will improve their living standards." Leaving aside whether the method is correct, let's talk about the facts. Now, the average worker only has sexual impulses and doesn't have sexual knowledge, and "sex" can be said to be the "only joyful enjoyment" of laborers. Therefore, not only is artificial control and regulation impossible, it is simply impossible. We can only treat Mr. Chen's theory as empty talk. There are special ways to improve workers' lives.

Improving the Environment

"Our nation lives and breathes in this difficult and distressing social environment, and maintaining life is already not easy... What use is it to insist on increasing births? Why don't we use birth control to improve the Chinese social environment?" This is the main idea of the fourth paragraph of the speech. It is a fact that the general people of China are in a difficult and distressing environment, but it is also a one-sided view to control births to improve the environment. Whether the social environment is good or bad depends entirely on the economic conditions at the time. Most people are busy year-round earning a living, or are unemployed and waiting to die. Even if they can control births, where do they have the time and ability to engage in "cultural," "academic," or "career" advancement? Moreover, as I said earlier, it is very difficult for people who are exhausted from labor to practice birth control!

National Health

"The health of children depends on the health of the mother. According to medical judgment, after a woman has given birth once, it takes at least three years to recover her health. Therefore, she should have another child at least every three years or more." On this point, I do not have deep medical knowledge and dare not make reckless judgments. However, facts and common sense tell me that it does not seem to require that long of a time. Even if we implement birth control according to Mr. Chen's judgment, but the country's sanitary facilities are like this, and human affairs are like that, even if Chinese children can bring a healthy physique from birth, I am afraid that not all of them will grow up healthy!

Mr. Chen's speech is entirely based on his own living environment. He is a preacher of determinism and can also be said to be a follower of Malthus. However, Malthus's "Principle of Population" has been criticized by informed people as "shallow and in the tone of a monk," and Professor Chen seems to admire Malthus very much. I dare not belittle Mr. Chen here. In the past, even Da Vinci and other scholars were often fooled by Malthus. In short, we firmly believe that if China does not overthrow imperialism and eradicate feudal forces, even if the population is reduced to the birth rate of Ireland, or even less, the result will only accelerate China's demise. As for birth control for people with venereal diseases, certain infectious diseases, or frailty, it should of course be practiced. These people should not only be made to abstain from sex but should also have their libido surgically removed. In addition, birth control for personal career or academic pursuits is a common phenomenon in civilized society. However, this cannot be regarded as a "national policy." Before humanity has invented other methods of reproduction, birth control can only be regarded as an individualistic and reluctant behavior. Why is there a need to loudly advocate it? What does Mr. Chen think?

Fish Language Understanding

Nursing my body covered in wounds, I am lost in thought: For the sake of a watery mirage, mistaking it for the gates of the Crystal Palace, I kept chasing, kept searching, and unconsciously entered the nets set by people. When I realized it, in order to win back my original freedom, I struggled several times, which is why I am now covered in wounds. But even so, I have strengthened my heart. As long as I can pierce this net and swim freely, I would gladly try even if it means my body is shattered to pieces. My companions in the net! Do not be sad or resentful anymore. Do not feel sorry. As long as you unite your strength and move forward! In the same direction!

Opinions of Great Thinkers of the World on Women's Issues (9) 281

— Hua

VII Owen (continued)

Regarding Owen's ideal society of gender equality, we briefly discussed it last time. Now let us describe his sharp criticism of modern marriage and family. Owen believes that compulsory marriage is the cause of family misfortune. In this kind of misfortune, women suffer particularly severely, and children morally degenerate as a result. He believes that prostitution is a result of hypocritical "church" marriages. Owen once said:

"Mankind has been a slave to the three major evils of today - private property, blind religious systems, and marriage based on the former two. The ever-increasing pursuit of wealth and the resulting marriage are gradually moving us further and further away from our nature and causing us to reach a state of decline physically and mentally. ... Modern marriage is merely a sinister fabrication of the clergy to make the people dependent on the unnatural laws of the state and the church. This union made by the clergy only gives the rich the opportunity to unite with the rich. In all modern societies, even merchants are no exception, there is no such hypocrisy and deception in this relationship between husband and wife.

They are all saying that women's chastity can only be guaranteed by the statutory slavery determined in marriage. But it can be said with great confidence that women's chastity can only be guaranteed after the current form of marriage is eliminated. At that time, could prostitution still be so prevalent as it is today?"

In Europe more than a hundred years ago, marriage was entirely controlled and dominated by the clergy. The wedding ceremony had to be held in a church, the harm of which was no less than the old Chinese saying, "the command of parents and the words of a matchmaker." Therefore, Owen had such a profound and sharp criticism. Secondly, Owen criticized modern families as follows:

"The family develops a selfish emotion in the hearts of children, teaching children to regard their own family as a small world, in which they repeat, 'My house, my wife, my property, my children, my husband...'

Therefore, in addition to advocating a fundamental change in the modern social organization, Owen asserted that it was necessary to improve family relations. He speculated that only a full public life can break the selfish and closed life of the current family system. He said:

"The residents of the new world must live together and eat in public dining halls; eliminate individual houses and replace them with large public dormitories; neither individuals nor families can have private property; everyone is a member of the community; everyone shares the public wealth - the fruits of public labor, regardless of status. At that time, women will enjoy the same rights as men, so their status will naturally be completely independent. Children belong to the commune, not the parents. As a result of the complete elimination of useless occupations and wasteful extravagance, the productive forces will increase greatly, and the social wealth will increase sharply. At that time, all considerations that restrict births will be unnecessary. Of course, at that time, society will pay attention to the appropriate combination of the two sexes in order to prevent the transmission of diseases to children or the proliferation of inferior races."

Owen vigorously advocated public education for children. His proposed method was: "Children must enter school from the age of three, eat in public dining halls, and live in public dormitories; but parents can visit and talk at any time. In school, children must acquire all necessary and beneficial knowledge; at that time, we must try our best to prevent children from acquiring various bad habits from their parents or by other means; at the same time, we must give children hints of good habits and hobbies, so that they tend towards a happy life and become useful members of society." Finally, Owen said about the future occupation of women: "In the future, the first occupation of women is to take care of children and their own homes; the second is to cultivate gardens and plant vegetables needed for public dining halls; the third is to undertake textile work suitable for women; the fourth is to make clothes for staff; and the fifth is to take turns working in public dining halls and public dormitories. At that time, women themselves will be well-educated, and they can also supervise some parts of children's education in schools."

However, Owen, like other utopian socialists (such as Fourier), flew high in the clouds of pure theory, simply describing his ideals, without building a bridge to the hell on earth, and without considering the realistic state of society and its dynamics. In other words, he did not indicate how to cross from the hell on earth to the paradise. Therefore, Owen's demands and teachings are not suitable as slogans for mobilizing the masses to fight for the cause of women's liberation.

Commemorating Lu Yin 282

— Fei

The "May Fourth" angry tide once surged up many beautiful and bright waves. Lu Yin, needless to say, was one of those waves, but she did not follow the tide and flow thousands of miles, but stagnated in a bay of water!

Really, a long time ago, I already had such a feeling: "Our writer - Lu Yin, is a little old!"

However, in today's reversal of the tide of "women returning to the family" and "good wife and loving mother doctrine," Lu Yin suddenly died! Alas! In the atmosphere of "not allowing women to be human," we have once again lost such a woman who "strives to be human"! It is too infuriating! The more I think about it, the more I admire and mourn Lu Yin! So when Factory Hidden was put into a coffin, I ran to attend her funeral.

The funeral was Christian. After everyone silently offered their tears, in the atmosphere of hymns of praise to God, Bible readings and prayers, and the pastor's sermon, her - Lu Yin's relatives and friends, said that the ritual was Lu Yin's will; how she had religious feelings and conformed to the words and deeds of religious figures; and her virtue in dealing with people; she was simply a typical good wife and loving mother with religious beliefs - although at that time, a reader of Lu Yin was dissatisfied with this distortion of Lu Yin, and stood up to point out Lu Yin's "anti-patriarchal" and "anti-feudal" spirit of "striving to be human," and that the will was a kind of "persistence in life" and not a religious belief! But I still can't help but appeal for our writer again!

Anyone who knows Lu Yin's life knows that she did receive religious education and was baptized when she was a child, but she rebelled against religion when she reached middle school! During the "May Fourth" era, she was one of the most famous leaders of the Beijing Student Union! Her words and deeds, her works, all fully demonstrated her spirit of opposing the old society and opposing the old ideas - the old etiquette! Take her love story, for example, it was also very bold and thorough - after Guo Mengliang died, she ran to Guo's house to commit suicide for love and spent more than a year, and finally escaped the constraints of the large family and fell in love with "little lover"! So although she did not move forward with the times, at least she took off the coat of a slave and had the will to be a human being!

Let us try to find her thoughts in her posthumous works: there is no need to turn them far away, just take the two articles that everyone sees now: In the article "Dream," she wrote at the end: "Lu Yina is holding a steel axe and hacking at the thorns. The sharp thorns hurt her fingers and toes, and drops of blood stained her skirt red; but she has vaguely seen the distant path shining, so she no longer cares about the arrogance of the god of fate, she only takes a belief in finding a way out and goes forward."

There is also such a passage in "The Tears of a Girl": "Yes, you are very sympathetic, this is the greatest emotion of mankind, but you are really too childish, this is a fact, do you want to solve it with your tears? Children, maybe you are right, you want to wash away the sins of the world with warm tears of sympathy, ... but the truth of this world has long been conquered by all the evil forces, therefore, it is useless to cry for her." From this, it can be seen that although she has not made much progress, she has never retreated! She only cared about straightening her spine and raising her head to be a human being during her lifetime.

Theft 283

— Yi Ming

One morning, a theft was discovered in the dormitory.

The victims were several ladies living on the second floor. Some of them had lost their parents, and some even had no siblings and were in charge of their families. Therefore, in addition to more than a hundred yuan, some important items were also lost this time.

Theft has a short history here. It is said that similar things happened last year, and the thief was actually a lady with a high status. Unfortunately, she was discovered, and the school authorities had to quietly notify her parents. Then, she was taken away silently, without any sound.

But this time it was a bit different, perhaps because the matter was serious? The news spread quickly, and it quickly entered everyone's ears, so everyone held fresh, curious feelings and looked forward to a fresh result. Piles of flies also buzzed: the fat dormitory supervisor shook her whole body of Ling flesh and walked busily. She threw a smile at every female student who came to greet her, followed by the same sentence:

"I'm going to check your rooms today, oh!" Her voice seemed to contain infinite apologies, and at the same time, she seemed to be hinting that the thief should quickly hide the things to avoid being searched by her. Following the announcement of the search and the temporary ban on students leaving the dormitory, the search did not begin until darkness ruled the earth. Naturally, the nanny's room had been searched, and every seam of every piece of clothing and every corner of every quilt was not easily let go, but still no evidence could be found. At this time, no one knew who was stealing and who was not, only the suspected nanny and "she" knew.

The thief was obviously not a man. Although female students can go out very freely at any time; can be held by their boyfriends and spin to the music of "Goodnight, Vienna" all night, the internal ban is very strict, and even a male dog is not allowed to pass by on weekdays.

Finally, the detective came, and everyone seemed to feel more interested. Curiosity was in everyone's chest, as if someone had thrown a stone into still water, and the round ripples were expanding on the lake surface. At that time, I, like the rest of the people, was in that mood and went into the room. I saw the detective carefully examining the box that had been dug out with a knife, and then said to the nanny next to him, "Bring your keys!" The nanny brought the keys from her own room. The detective then picked out one from the bunch, inserted it into the lock, and turned it. The lock opened with a bang.

"What else do you have to say? The money proves that you stole it!" The detective showed a smug grin and said to the stunned nanny.

"Sir, I didn't steal it..." Before she finished speaking, the detective waved the key in front of her face and then said:

"Didn't steal it? What is this?"

"Sir, I really didn't steal it. The keys happen to be the same. If I stole it, why didn't I throw it away earlier? Since I have a key to open it, why use force to dig it?"

"That's a trap you set, who knows? In short, you are the only poor person here; people do bad things when they are poor... Could it be that the ladies here would steal? They eat well and dress well, have a lot of their own money, and still want other people's money? Only poor people are willing to risk their lives for money!" "Don't say that, sir! Although I am poor, my heart is very pure." Poor people do not necessarily do bad things; there are many bad things that poor people cannot do!

"Stole the money and still talking back?" I don't know why the detective became ashamed and angry. "You must have stolen the money! ... Okay, I'll give you three days to hand over the things, otherwise, I won't be polite and you'll have to come to the line with me!"

"I really didn't steal it," the nanny still insisted, "It's no use forcing me to go to jail and suffer. Anyway, I only have an old life to risk... I'm pitiful and lonely..." After hearing about the jail sentence three days later, a sense of tragic life that had been covered by excessive labor for a long time now jumped into her heart: old tears could not help but roll down like broken beads.

This scene tore my mind, I covered my face and escaped from the crowd; the nanny's tears fell on my heart like frying oil. Yes, she was right. There are many bad things in the world that poor people cannot do; and there are many vicious hearts that are rare among poor people! The nanny herself is an example. She knows that she did not steal, and she usually serves the ladies faithfully like cattle and horses, but as a result, she has become someone else's scapegoat. Maybe she is a scapegoat for a wealthy lady who is being served by her!

Imagining what she would be like three days later; imagining the scene of her being whipped when she had nothing to confess, I seemed to clearly hear her miserable cry. I couldn't help but cover my ears, but the sound seemed to be expanding towards me, becoming many tragic cries..."
